\Hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1029}%
 All notable changes to the input system package will be documented in this file.

The format is based on \href{http://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/}{\texttt{ Keep a Changelog}} and this project adheres to \href{http://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html}{\texttt{ Semantic Versioning}}.

Due to package verification, the latest version below is the unpublished version and the date is meaningless. however, it has to be formatted properly to pass verification tests.\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1030}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+6.\+3\mbox{]} -\/ 2023-\/07-\/11}{\mbox{[}1.\+6.\+3\mbox{]} -\/ 2023-\/07-\/11}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1030}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Enabled {\ttfamily display\+Index} support for \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} 2022.\+3.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1034}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1034}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed UI clicks not registering when OS provides multiple input sources for the same event, e.\+g. on Samsung Dex (case ISX-\/1416, ISXB-\/342).
\item Fixed unstable integration test {\ttfamily Integration\+\_\+\+Can\+Send\+And\+Receive\+Events} by ignoring application focus on integration tests. (case ISX-\/1381)
\item Fixed broken "{}\+Listen"{} button in Input actions editor window with \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} dark skin (case ISXB-\/536).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1035}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+6.\+1\mbox{]} -\/ 2023-\/05-\/26}{\mbox{[}1.\+6.\+1\mbox{]} -\/ 2023-\/05-\/26}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1035}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1036}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1036}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed issue with compiling in \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} 2022.\+1 and with XR Toolkit by guarding the experimental UITK Asset Editor code completely.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1037}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+6.\+0\mbox{]} -\/ 2023-\/05-\/25}{\mbox{[}1.\+6.\+0\mbox{]} -\/ 2023-\/05-\/25}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1037}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1038}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1038}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added internal {\ttfamily Input\+System\+Provider} class for the new {\ttfamily Input\+For\+UI} internal module. {\ttfamily Input\+For\+UI} allows the UIToolkit to have a single dependency for input events, regardless of using the new input system or the legacy input system.
\item Added {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+custom\+Binding\+Path\+Validators} interface to allow showing warnings in the {\ttfamily Input\+Asset} Editor for specific Input\+Bindings and draw custom UI in the properties panel.
\item Added {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+run\+In\+Background} to be used internally by specific platforms packages. Allows telling the input system that a specific platform runs in background. It allows fixing of \href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/UUM-6744}{\texttt{ case UUM-\/6744}}.
\item Added new UIToolkit version of the {\ttfamily Input\+Actions\+Asset} editor. Currently this is incomplete (view-\/only) and the existing editor is still used by default.
\item Added {\ttfamily display\+Index} field to the Touch struct to expose the index of the display that was touched.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1039}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1039}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Changed XR Layout build behavior to create Axis2D control devices with {\ttfamily Stick\+Control} type instead of {\ttfamily Vector2\+Control}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1040}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1040}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed Binding\+Path String-\/\+Comparison to be culture and case insensitive (case ISXB-\/449).
\item Fixed custom processor display in the input action asset UI after entering/exiting play mode (previously they got hidden) (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-445}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/445}}).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1041}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+5.\+1\mbox{]} -\/ 2023-\/03-\/15}{\mbox{[}1.\+5.\+1\mbox{]} -\/ 2023-\/03-\/15}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1041}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1042}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1042}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed unclosed profiler marker in {\ttfamily Invoke\+Callbacks\+Safe\+\_\+\+Any\+Callback\+Returns\+True} which would lead to eventually broken profiler traces in some cases like using {\ttfamily Player\+Input} (case ISXB-\/393).
\item Fixed Input\+Action.\+bindings.\+count not getting correctly updated after removing bindings with Erase().
\item Fixed an issue where connecting a gamepad in the editor with certain settings will cause memory and performance to degrade (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/UUM-19480}{\texttt{ case UUM-\/19480}}).
\item Fixed issue leading to a stack overflow crash during device initialization in {\ttfamily Insert\+Control\+Bit\+Range\+Node} (case ISXB-\/405).
\item Fixed the issue where saving and loading override bindings to JSON would set unassigned overrides (that were {\ttfamily null}) to assigned overrides (as an empty string {\ttfamily "{}"{}}).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1043}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+5.\+0\mbox{]} -\/ 2023-\/01-\/24}{\mbox{[}1.\+5.\+0\mbox{]} -\/ 2023-\/01-\/24}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1043}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1044}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1044}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added support for reading Tracking State in \href{xref:UnityEngine.InputSystem.XR.TrackedPoseDriver}{\texttt{ Tracked\+Pose\+Driver}} to constrain whether the input pose is applied to the Transform. This should be used when the device supports valid flags for the position and rotation values, which is the case for XR poses.
\item Added {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+shortcut\+Keys\+Consume\+Input}. This allows programmatic access to opt-\/in to the enhanced shortcut key behaviour (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-254}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/254}})).
\item Significantly optimized cost of {\ttfamily Read\+Value}/{\ttfamily Read\+Unprocessed\+Value\+From\+State}/{\ttfamily Write\+Value\+Into\+State} for some control types. Optimization is opt-\/in for now, please call {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+settings.\+Set\+Internal\+Feature\+Flag("{}\+USE\+\_\+\+OPTIMIZED\+\_\+\+CONTROLS"{}, true);} in your project to enable it. You can observe which controls are optimized by looking at new optimized column in device debugger. You will need to call a new {\ttfamily Input\+Control.\+Apply\+Parameter\+Changes()} method if the code is changing {\ttfamily Axis\+Control} fields after initial setup is done.
\item Added the ability to change the origin positioning and movement behaviour of the On\+Screen\+Stick ({\ttfamily On\+Screen\+Stick.\+cs}) via the new {\ttfamily behaviour} property. This currently supports three modes of operation, two of which are new in addition to the previous behaviour. Based on the user contribution from \href{https://github.com/eblabs}{\texttt{ eblabs}} in \href{https://github.com/Unity-Technologies/InputSystem/pull/658}{\texttt{ \#658}}.
\item Significantly optimized cost of {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Read\+Value} and {\ttfamily Input\+Control.\+Read\+Value} calls by introducing caching behaviour to input controls. Input controls now keep track of whether their underlying state has been changed and only read the value from the underlying state and apply processors when absolutely necessary. Optimization is opt-\/in for now, please call {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+settings.\+Set\+Internal\+Feature\+Flag("{}\+USE\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+VALUE\+\_\+\+CACHING"{}, true);} in your project to enable it. If there are issues try enabling {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+settings.\+Set\+Internal\+Feature\+Flag("{}\+PARANOID\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+VALUE\+\_\+\+CACHING\+\_\+\+CHECKS"{}, true);} and check in the console if there are any errors regarding caching.
\item Added a note in the \doxysectlink{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_documentation_0i_2_supported_devices}{supported devices page}{0} about Dual\+Sense support for Android devices.
\item Exposed {\ttfamily display\+Index} property for {\ttfamily Pointer}, {\ttfamily Touchscreen}, {\ttfamily Touch\+Control}, {\ttfamily Touch\+State}, {\ttfamily Mouse}, {\ttfamily Mouse\+State} which enables look up of the logical screen associated with a pointer event via (display documentation)\mbox{[}\href{https://docs.unity3d.com/ScriptReference/Display.html}{\texttt{ https\+://docs.\+unity3d.\+com/\+Script\+Reference/\+Display.\+html}}\mbox{]}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1045}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1045}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed composite bindings incorrectly getting a control scheme assigned when pasting into input asset editor with a control scheme selected.
\item Fixed an issue on PS5 where device disconnected events that happen while the app is in the background are missed causing orphaned devices to hang around forever and exceptions when the same device is added again (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/UUM-6744}{\texttt{ case UUM-\/7842}}).
\item Fixed Switch Pro, Dual\+Shock 4, Dual\+Sense gamepads becoming current on PC/mac\+OS when no controls are changing (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-223}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/223}})).
\item Fixed an issue that made On\+Screen\+Stick unusable when used in conjunction with Player\+Input in Auto-\/\+Switch devices mode, or with any code that changes user/device pairing on unsued device activity being detected (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-48}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/48}}).
\item Fixed issue where input events were being suppressed during interactive action rebinding even when when their controls were excluded (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/mouse-position-and-mouse-click-input-not-recognized-when-rebinding-is-active}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/367}}).
\item Removed unneeded check that could trigger a Not\+Implemented\+Exception when binding to a Usage (e.\+g. Submit) (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-373}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/373}}).
\item Display a warning instead of throwing a Not\+Implemented\+Exception when loading binding overrides from json when some of the entries have become outdated (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-375}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/375}}).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1046}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1046}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Extended input action code generator ({\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Code\+Generator.\+cs}) to support optional registration and unregistration of callbacks for multiple callback instances via {\ttfamily Add\+Callbacks(...)} and {\ttfamily Remove\+Callbacks(...)} part of the generated code. Contribution by \href{https://github.com/Ramobo}{\texttt{ Ramobo}} in \href{https://github.com/Unity-Technologies/InputSystem/pull/889}{\texttt{ \#889}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1047}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1047}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Changed define requirements of {\ttfamily Unity.\+Input\+System.\+Test\+Framework}, so that it can be used by other packages without setting the {\ttfamily com.\+unity.\+inputsystem} package to be testable in the project manifest.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1048}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+4.\+4\mbox{]} -\/ 2022-\/11-\/01}{\mbox{[}1.\+4.\+4\mbox{]} -\/ 2022-\/11-\/01}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1048}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1049}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1049}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Argument\+Null\+Exception} when opening the Prefab Overrides window and selecting a component with an {\ttfamily Input\+Action}.
\item Fixed {\ttfamily \{file\+ID\+: 0\}} getting appended to {\ttfamily Project\+Settings.\+asset} file when building a project (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-296}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/296}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Type of instance in array does not match expected type} assertion when using Player\+Input in combination with Control Schemes and Interactions (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-282}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/282}}).
\item The {\ttfamily Input\+Actions consume their inputs} behaviour for shortcut support introduced in v1.\+4 is opt-\/in now and can be enabled via the project settings (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-254}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/254}})).
\item Fixed Memory alignment issue with deserialized Input\+Event\+Traces that could cause infinite loops when playing back replays (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-317}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/317}}).
\item Fixed an Invalid\+Operation\+Exception when using Hold interaction, and by extension any interaction that changes to performed state after a timeout (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-330}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/332}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Given object is neither an Input\+Action nor an Input\+Action\+Map} when using {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Trace} on input action from an input action asset (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-29}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/29}}).
\item Fixing devices not being removed if unplugged during domain reload (entering or exiting play mode) (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-232}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/232}}).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1050}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+4.\+3\mbox{]} -\/ 2022-\/09-\/23}{\mbox{[}1.\+4.\+3\mbox{]} -\/ 2022-\/09-\/23}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1050}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1051}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1051}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added missing script and gizmo icon for {\ttfamily Tracked\+Pose\+Driver.\+cs} component (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-262}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/262}}).
\item Fix for mitigating symptoms reported in (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/UUM-10774}{\texttt{ case UUM-\/10774}} effectively avoiding reenabling mouse, pen or touch devices in {\ttfamily Input\+System\+Plugin.\+On\+Destroy()} if currently quitting the editor. The fix avoids editor crashing if closed when Simulator Window is open. Note that the actual issue needs a separate fix in \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} and this package fix is only to avoid running into the issue.
\item Fixed an issue where Input Action name would not display correctly in Inspector if serialized as {\ttfamily \mbox{[}Serialized\+Property\mbox{]}} within a class not derived from {\ttfamily Mono\+Behavior} (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-124}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/124}}.
\item Fix an issue where users could end up with the wrong device assignments when using the Input\+User API directly and removing a user (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-231}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/274}}).
\item Fixed an issue where Player\+Input behavior description was not updated when changing action assset (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-286}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/286}}).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1052}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1052}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Readded On\+Disable() member to Multiplayer\+Event\+System which was previously removed from the API
\item Improved performance of HID descriptor parsing by moving json parsing to a simple custom predicitve parser instead of relying on \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity}\textquotesingle{}s json parsing. This should improve domain reload times when there are many HID devices connected to a machine.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1053}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1053}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Documentation improvements\+: New workflows and concepts pages. Reorganised table of contents. Improved some code samples. Updated screenshots.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1054}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+4.\+2\mbox{]} -\/ 2022-\/08-\/12}{\mbox{[}1.\+4.\+2\mbox{]} -\/ 2022-\/08-\/12}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1054}
