\item Hide XR legacy HMD and controllers layouts from Editor UI dropdown.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1056}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1056}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fix UI sometimes ignoring the first mouse click event after losing and regaining focus (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-127}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/127}}.
\item Fixed issue when using Multiplayer\+Event\+Systems where the visual state of UI controls would change due to constant toggling of Canvas\+Group.\+interactable on and off (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-112}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/112}}).
\item Fixed minor issue when renaming input actions where unique renaming would incorrectly consider the input action being renamed as a different action and not allow renaming of \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{} to \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{} without appending a unique integer for example (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-25}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/25}}).
\item Fixed an issue where the Input Action asset icon would not be visible during asset creation (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-6}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/6}}).
\item Fixed Dual\+Sense low frequency motor speed being always set to min value.
\item Fixed an issue where {\ttfamily Read\+Unprocessed\+Value\+From\+State} in Pose\+Control always returning default values.
\item Fix \doxylink{class_player}{Player} 1\textquotesingle{}s UI controls stop working after second player joins (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-125}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/125}}))
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1057}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+4.\+1\mbox{]} -\/ 2022-\/05-\/30}{\mbox{[}1.\+4.\+1\mbox{]} -\/ 2022-\/05-\/30}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1057}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1058}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1058}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed composite touchscreen controls were not firing an action if screen was touched before enabling the action (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/ISXB-98}{\texttt{ case ISXB-\/98}}).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1059}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+4.\+0\mbox{]} -\/ 2022-\/04-\/10}{\mbox{[}1.\+4.\+0\mbox{]} -\/ 2022-\/04-\/10}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1059}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1060}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1060}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Button} type {\ttfamily Input\+Action}s now go to {\ttfamily started} when a button goes from a press to below the release threshold but not yet to 0. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Before:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{Set(Gamepad.current.rightTrigger,\ 0.7f);\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Performed\ (pressed)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{Set(Gamepad.current.rightTrigger,\ 0.2f);\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Canceled\ (released)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{Set(Gamepad.current.rightTrigger,\ 0.1f);\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Started!!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{Set(Gamepad.current.rightTrigger,\ 0f);\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Canceled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Now:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{Set(Gamepad.current.rightTrigger,\ 0.7f);\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Performed\ (pressed)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{Set(Gamepad.current.rightTrigger,\ 0.2f);\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Started\ (released\ but\ not\ fully)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{Set(Gamepad.current.rightTrigger,\ 0.1f);\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ <Nothing>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{Set(Gamepad.current.rightTrigger,\ 0f);\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Canceled}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This also applies to {\ttfamily Press\+Interaction} when set to {\ttfamily Press} behavior.
\item In effect, it means that a button will be in {\ttfamily started} or {\ttfamily performed} phase for as long as its value is not 0 and will only go to {\ttfamily canceled} once dropping to 0.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Processors are now always applied when reading action values through {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Read\+Value\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} or {\ttfamily Callback\+Context.\+Read\+Value\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}. Previously, if no bound control was actuated, Read\+Value calls would return the default value for the action type but not run the value through the processors.(\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/1293728/}{\texttt{ case 1293728}}).
\item Made the following internal types public. These types can be useful when deconstructing raw events captured via {\ttfamily Input\+Event\+Trace}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Unity\+Engine.\+Input\+System.\+Android.\+Low\+Level.\+Android\+Axis}
\item {\ttfamily Unity\+Engine.\+Input\+System.\+Android.\+Low\+Level.\+Android\+Game\+Controller\+State}
\item {\ttfamily Unity\+Engine.\+Input\+System.\+Android.\+Low\+Level.\+Android\+Key\+Code}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Adding or removing a device no longer leads to affected actions being temporarily disabled (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputactionreferences-reading-resets-when-inputactionmap-has-an-action-for-the-other-hand-and-that-hand-starts-slash-stops-tracking}{\texttt{ case 1379932}}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If, for example, an action was bound to {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Gamepad\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}/button\+South} and was enabled, adding a second {\ttfamily Gamepad} would lead to the action being temporarily disabled, then updated, and finally re-\/enabled.
\item This was especially noticeable if the action was currently in progress as it would get cancelled and then subsequently resumed.
\item Now, an in-\/progress action will get cancelled if the device of its active control is removed. If its active control is not affected, however, the action will keep going regardless of whether controls are added or removed from its {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+controls} list.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Installing the package for the first time will now set {\ttfamily "{}\+Active Input Handling"{}} to {\ttfamily "{}\+Both"{}} rather than {\ttfamily "{}\+Input System Package"{}}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This means, that by default, both the old and the new input system will run side by side where supported.
\item This can be manually switched by going to {\ttfamily Edit \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} Project Settings \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \doxylink{class_player}{Player} \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} Active Input Handling}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1061}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1061}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed an issue where a layout-\/override registered via {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Register\+Layout\+Override(...)} would cause the editor to malfunction or crash if the layout override had a name already used by an existing layout (case 1377685).
\item Fixed an issue where attempting to replace an existing layout-\/override by using an existing layout-\/override name didn\textquotesingle{}t work as expected and would instead aggregate overrides instead of replacing them when an override with the given name already exists.
\item Fixed Switch Pro controller not working correctly in different scenarios (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/nintendo-switch-pro-controller-output-garbage}{\texttt{ case 1369091}}, \href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputsystem-windows-switch-pro-controller-only-works-when-connected-via-bluetooth-but-not-via-usb}{\texttt{ case 1190216}}, case 1314869).
\item Fixed Dual\+Shock 4 controller not allowing input from other devices due to noisy input from its unmapped sensors (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-from-the-keyboard-is-not-working-when-the-dualshock-4-controller-is-connected}{\texttt{ case 1365891}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+on\+Any\+Button\+Press} so that it doesn\textquotesingle{}t throw exceptions when trying to process non state or delta events (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/1376034/}{\texttt{ case 1376034}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+Control\+Path.\+Matches} incorrectly reporting matches when only a prefix was matching.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This would, for example, cause {\ttfamily Keyboard.\+e\+Key} to be matched by {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Keyboard\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}/escape}.
\item Fix contributed by \href{https://github.com/steinbitglis}{\texttt{ Fredrik Ludvigsen}} in \href{https://github.com/Unity-Technologies/InputSystem/pull/1485}{\texttt{ \#1485}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily On\+Screen\+Button} triggering {\ttfamily Null\+Reference\+Exception} in combination with custom devices (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/nullreferenceexception-error-when-setting-on-screen-button-to-a-custom-device}{\texttt{ case 1380790}}).
\item Fixed no devices being available in {\ttfamily Start} and {\ttfamily Awake} methods if, in the player, any {\ttfamily Input\+System} API was accessed during the {\ttfamily Subsystem\+Registration} phase (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputsystem-does-not-initialize-properly-in-a-build-when-accessed-early}{\texttt{ case 1392358}}).
\item Fixed dropdown for "{}\+Supported Devices"{} in settings not showing all device layouts.
\item Fixed "{}\+STAT event with state format TOUC cannot be used with device \textquotesingle{}\+Touchscreen\+:/\+Touchscreen\textquotesingle{}"{} when more than max supported amount of fingers, currently 10, are present on the screen at a same time (case 1395648).
\item Fixed mouse events not being timesliced when input system is switched to process input in fixed updates (case 1386738).
\item Fixed missing tooltips in Player\+Input\+Manager\+Editor for the \doxylink{class_player}{Player} Limit and Fixed Splitscreen sizes labels (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/player-input-manager-pops-up-placeholder-text-when-hovering-over-it}{\texttt{ case 1396945}}).
\item Fixed Dual\+Shock 4 controllers not working in some scenarios by adding support for extended mode HID reports (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-dualshock4-controller-returns-random-input-values-when-connected-via-bluetooth-while-steam-is-running}{\texttt{ case 1281633}}, case 1409867).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Background\+Behavior.\+Ignore\+Focus} having no effect when {\ttfamily Application.\+run\+In\+Background} was false (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/xr-head-tracking-lost-when-lost-focus-with-action-based-trackedposedriver-on-android}{\texttt{ case 1400456}}).
\item Fixed an issue where a device was left disabled when it was disconnected while an application was out-\/of-\/focus and then re-\/connected when in-\/focus (case 1404320).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1062}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1062}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Invalid\+Cast\+Exception\+: Specified cast is not valid.} being thrown when clicking on menu separators in the control picker (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/invalidcastexception-is-thrown-when-selecting-the-header-of-an-advanceddropdown}{\texttt{ case 1388049}}).
\item Fixed accessing {\ttfamily Input\+Action}s directly during {\ttfamily Runtime\+Initialize\+On\+Load} not initializing the input system as a whole and leading to exceptions (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-nullreferenceexception-error-is-thrown-when-using-input-actions-in-builds}{\texttt{ case 1378614}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Get\+Timeout\+Completion\+Percentage} jumping to 100\% completion early (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/gettimeoutcompletionpercentage-returns-1-after-0-dot-1s-when-hold-action-was-started-even-though-it-is-not-performed-yet}{\texttt{ case 1377009}}).
\item Fixed d-\/pad inputs sometimes being ignored on actions that were binding to multiple controls (\href{https://unity.slack.com/archives/G01RVV1SPU4/p1642501574002300}{\texttt{ case 1389858}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Index\+Out\+Of\+Range\+Exception} when having multiple interactions on an action and/or binding in an action map other than the first of an asset (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/map-index-on-trigger-and-indexoutofrangeexception-are-thrown-when-using-interaction-on-both-binding-and-its-parent-action}{\texttt{ case 1392559}}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fix contributed by \href{https://github.com/russellquinn}{\texttt{ Russell Quinn}} in \href{https://github.com/Unity-Technologies/InputSystem/pull/1483}{\texttt{ \#1483}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Axis\+Composite} not respecting processors applied to {\ttfamily positive} and {\ttfamily negative} bindings (case 1398942).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This was a regression introduced in \doxylink{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_axiscomposite-min-max-value-fix}{1.0.0-\/pre.6}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed calling {\ttfamily action.\+Add\+Composite\+Binding(...).With(...)} while action is enabled not correctly updating controls for part bindings of the composite.
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Two\+Modifiers\+Composite} inadvertently not allowing controls other than {\ttfamily Button\+Control}s being bound to its {\ttfamily binding} part.
\item Added support for keyboard shortcuts and mutually exclusive use of modifiers.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item In short, this means that a "{}\+Shift+\+B"{} binding can now prevent a "{}\+B"{} binding from triggering.
\item {\ttfamily One\+Modifier\+Composite}, {\ttfamily Two\+Modifiers\+Composite}, as well as the legacy {\ttfamily Button\+With\+One\+Modifier\+Composite} and {\ttfamily Button\+With\+Two\+Modifiers\+Composite} now require their modifiers to be pressed {\bfseries{before}} (or at least simultaneously with) pressing the target button.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This check is performed only if the target is a button. For a binding such as {\ttfamily "{}\+CTRL+\+Mouse\+Delta"{}} the check is bypassed. It can also be manually bypassed via the {\ttfamily override\+Modifiers\+Need\+To\+Be\+Pressed\+First}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item State change monitors on a device ({\ttfamily IInput\+State\+Change\+Monitor}) are now sorted by their {\ttfamily monitor\+Index} and will trigger in that order.
\item Actions are now automatically arranging their bindings to trigger in the order of decreasing "{}complexity"{}. This metric is derived automatically. The more complex a composite a binding is part of, the higher its complexity. So, {\ttfamily "{}\+Shift+\+B"{}} has a higher "{}complexity"{} than just {\ttfamily "{}\+B"{}}.
\item If an binding of higher complexity "{}consumes"{} a given input, all bindings waiting to consume the same input will automatically get skipped. So, if a {\ttfamily "{}\+Shift+\+B"{}} binding composite consumes a {\ttfamily "{}\+B"{}} key press, a binding to {\ttfamily "{}\+B"{}} that is waiting in line will get skipped and not see the key press.
\item If your project is broken by these changes, you can disable the new behaviors via a feature toggle in code\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{InputSystem.settings.SetInternalFeatureFlag(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}DISABLE\_SHORTCUT\_SUPPORT"{}},\ \textcolor{keyword}{true});}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added new APIs for getting and setting parameter values on interactions, processors, and composites. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Get\ parameter.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{action.GetParameterValue(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}duration"{}});\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Any\ "{}duration"{}\ value\ on\ any\ binding.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{action.GetParameterValue(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}tap:duration"{}});\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ "{}duration"{}\ on\ "{}tap"{}\ interaction\ on\ any\ binding.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{action.GetParameterValue(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}tap:duration"{}},\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ "{}duration"{}\ on\ "{}tap"{}\ on\ binding\ in\ "{}Gamepad"{}\ group.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ InputBinding.MaskByGroup(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Gamepad"{}}));}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Set\ parameter.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{action.ApplyParameterOverride(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}duration"{}},\ 0.4f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{action.ApplyParameterOverride(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}tap:duration"{}},\ 0.4f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{action.ApplyParameterOverride(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}tap:duration"{}},\ 0.4f,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ InputBinding.MaskByGroup(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Gamepad"{}}));}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Can\ also\ apply\ parameter\ overrides\ at\ the\ level\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ InputActionMaps\ and\ InputActionAssets\ with\ an\ effect}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ on\ all\ the\ bindings\ contained\ therein.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{asset.ApplyParameterOverride(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}scaleVector2:x"{}},\ 0.25f,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{new}\ InputBinding(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}<Mouse>/delta"{}}));}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1063}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1063}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added support for "{}\+Hori Co HORIPAD for Nintendo Switch"{}, "{}\+HORI Pokken Tournament DX Pro Pad"{}, "{}\+HORI Wireless Switch Pad"{}, "{}\+HORI Real Arcade Pro V Hayabusa in Switch Mode"{}, "{}\+Power\+A NSW Fusion Wired Fight\+Pad"{}, "{}\+Power\+A NSW Fusion Pro Controller (\+USB only)"{}, "{}\+PDP Wired Fight Pad Pro\+: Mario"{}, "{}\+PDP Faceoff Wired Pro Controller for Nintendo Switch"{}, "{}\+PDP Faceoff Wired Pro Controller for Nintendo Switch"{}, "{}\+PDP Afterglow Wireless Switch Controller"{}, "{}\+PDP Rockcandy Wired Controller"{}.
\item Added support for Steel\+Series Nimbus+ gamepad on Mac (addition contributed by \href{https://github.com/MollyJameson}{\texttt{ Mollyjameson}}).
\item Added support for Game \doxylink{namespace_core}{Core} platforms to XR layouts, devices, and input controls. These classes were previously only enabled on platforms where {\ttfamily ENABLE\+\_\+\+VR} is defined.
\item Added a new {\ttfamily Delta\+Control} control type that is now used for delta-\/style controls such as {\ttfamily Mouse.\+delta} and {\ttfamily Mouse.\+scroll}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Like {\ttfamily Stick\+Control}, this control has individual {\ttfamily up}, {\ttfamily down}, {\ttfamily left}, and {\ttfamily right} controls (as well as {\ttfamily x} and {\ttfamily y} that it inherits from {\ttfamily Vector2\+Control}). This means it is now possible to directly bind to individual scroll directions (such as {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Mouse\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}/scroll/up}).
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added the \textquotesingle{}Cursor Lock Behavior\textquotesingle{} setting to Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module to control the origin point of UI raycasts when the cursor is locked. This enables the use of Physics\+Raycaster when the cursor is locked to the center of the screen (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/1395281/}{\texttt{ case 1395281}}).
\item Added support for using the \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} Remote app with the Input \doxylink{namespace_system}{System}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Requires \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} 2021.\+2.\+18 or later.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1064}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+3.\+0\mbox{]} -\/ 2021-\/12-\/10}{\mbox{[}1.\+3.\+0\mbox{]} -\/ 2021-\/12-\/10}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1064}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1065}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1065}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The artificial {\ttfamily ctrl}, {\ttfamily shift}, and {\ttfamily alt} controls (which combine the left and right controls into one) on the keyboard can now be written to and no longer throw {\ttfamily Not\+Supported\+Exception} when trying to do so (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/on-screen-button-errors-on-mouse-down-slash-up-when-its-control-path-is-set-to-control-keyboard}{\texttt{ case 1340793}}).
\item All devices are now re-\/synced/reset in next update after entering play mode, this is needed to read current state of devices before any intentional input is provided (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/mouse-coordinates-reported-as-00-until-the-first-move}{\texttt{ case 1231907}}).
\item Replaced {\ttfamily Unity\+Linker\+Build\+Pipeline\+Data.\+input\+Directory} with hardcoded {\ttfamily Temp} folder because {\ttfamily input\+Directory} is deprecated.
\item Deprecated {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+filter\+Noise\+On\+Current}. Now noise filtering is always enabled. Device only will become {\ttfamily .current} if any non-\/noise control have changed state.
\item A device reset (such as when focus is lost) on {\ttfamily Touchscreen} will now result in all ongoing touches getting cancelled instead of all touches being simply reset to default state.
\item Calling {\ttfamily Input\+Test\+Fixture.\+Press}, {\ttfamily Input\+Test\+Fixture.\+Set}, etc. from within a {\ttfamily \mbox{[}Unity\+Test\mbox{]}} will no longer immediately process input. Instead, input will be processed like it normally would as part of the \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} player loop.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1066}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1066}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed writing values into the half-\/axis controls of sticks (such as {\ttfamily Gamepad.\+left\+Stick.\+left}) producing incorrect values on the stick (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputtestfixture-tests-return-inverted-values-when-pressing-gamepads-left-or-down-joystick-buttons}{\texttt{ case 1336240}}).
\item Fixed setting size of event trace in input debugger always growing back to largest size set before.
\item Fixed successive clicks not getting triggered with {\ttfamily Touch\+Simulation} on when not moving the mouse in-\/between clicks (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/onclick-isnt-triggered-on-the-second-click-when-the-mouse-isnt-moved-and-simulate-touch-input-from-mouse-or-pen-is-enabled}{\texttt{ case 1330014}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} stopping to listen for input when swapping {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Asset} instances while input was disabled (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/ui-navigation-stops-working-after-adding-two-input-devices-to-a-scene}{\texttt{ case 1371332}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} showing incorrect bindings after pressing the \textquotesingle{}Fix UI Input Module\textquotesingle{} button in Player\+Input component(\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/1319968/}{\texttt{ case 1319968}}).
\item Fixed an issue where UI button clicks could be ignored by {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} if modifying on-\/screen devices from Update() callbacks (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/1365070}{\texttt{ case 1365070}}).
\item Fixed an issue with {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} that would cause UI to stop responding during play mode after changing a script file while Recompile and Continue mode is active, or by forcing a script recompile using {\ttfamily Request\+Script\+Compilation}(\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/1324215/}{\texttt{ case 1324215}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} inspector showing all action bindings as "{}\+None"{} when assigned a runtime created actions asset (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-ui-input-module-loses-prefab-action-mapping-in-local-co-op}{\texttt{ case 1304943}}).
\item Fixed a problem with UI Toolkit buttons remaining active when multiple fingers are used on a touchscreen, using {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} with pointer\+Behavior set to {\ttfamily UIPointer\+Behavior.\+Single\+Unified\+Pointer}. UI Toolkit will now always receive the same pointer\+Id when that option is in use, regardless of the hardware component that produced the pointer event. (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/transitions-get-stuck-when-pointer-behavior-is-set-to-single-unified-pointer-and-multiple-touches-are-made}{\texttt{ case 1369081}}).
\item Fixed a problem with {\ttfamily Input\+User} where devices would be removed and not added again after layout overrides preventing certain devices, e.\+g. gamepads to not work correctly when associated with action map bindings tied to {\ttfamily Player\+Input} (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/1347320}{\texttt{ case 1347320}}).
\item Fixed Dual\+Sense on i\+OS not inheriting from {\ttfamily Dual\+Shock\+Gamepad} (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-dualsense-detection-ios}{\texttt{ case 1378308}}).
\item Fixed a device becoming {\ttfamily .current} (e.\+g. {\ttfamily Gamepad.\+current}, etc) when sending a new state event that contains no control changes (case 1377952).
\item Fixed calling {\ttfamily Is\+Pressed} on an entire device returning {\ttfamily true} (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputcontrol-dot-ispressed-always-returns-true-when-using-new-input-system}{\texttt{ case 1374024}}).
\item Fixed HIDs having blackslashes in their vendor or product names leading to binding paths generated by interactive rebinding that failed to resolve to controls and thus lead to no input being received (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/1335465/}{\texttt{ case 1335465}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Register\+Layout\+Override} resulting in the layout that overrides are being applied to losing the connection to its base layout (\href{https://fogbugz.unity3d.com/f/cases/1377719/}{\texttt{ case 1377719}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Touch.\+active\+Touches} still registering touches after the app loses focus (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-new-input-system-registering-active-touches-when-app-loses-focus}{\texttt{ case 1364017}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Multiplayer\+Event\+System} not preventing keyboard and gamepad/joystick navigation from one player\textquotesingle{}s UI moving to another player\textquotesingle{}s UI (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-ui-input-module-lets-the-player-navigate-across-other-canvases}{\texttt{ case 1306361}}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This fix relies on a {\ttfamily Canvas\+Group} being injected into each {\ttfamily player\+Root} and the {\ttfamily interactable} property of the group being toggled back and forth depending on which part of the UI is being updated.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+Test\+Fixture} incorrectly running input updates out of sync with the player loop (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/buttoncontrol-dot-waspressedthisframe-is-false-when-using-inputtestfixture-dot-press}{\texttt{ case 1341740}}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This had effects such as {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Was\+Pressed\+This\+Frame()} returning false expectedly.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed broken code example for state structs in {\ttfamily Devices.\+md} documentation (fix contributed by \href{https://github.com/jeffreylanters}{\texttt{ jeffreylanters}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Tracked\+Device\+Raycaster} not picking closest hit in scene (fix originally contributed by \href{https://github.com/alexboost222}{\texttt{ alexboost222}}).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1067}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1067}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed opening a new project (or one that needs a full reimport) leading to several exceptions in the console if the most recently opened project was closed with a {\ttfamily .inputactions} editor open (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/exceptions-about-previously-open-action-map-being-thrown-when-opening-new-project}{\texttt{ case 1313185}}).
\item Fixed incorrect indentation of input actions in the inspector (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/1285546/}{\texttt{ case 1285546}}).
\item Fixed an issue where serialized {\ttfamily Input\+Action} properties would have display name "{}\+Input Action"{} in the Inspector window instead of their given name. (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/1367240}{\texttt{ case 1367240}}).
\item Fixed an issue where {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Enable} would not reuse memory allocated prior and thus lead to memory leaks (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-puts-a-lot-of-pressure-on-the-garbage-collector-when-enabling-and-disabling-inputactionmaps}{\texttt{ case 1367442}}).
\item Fixed interactions such as {\ttfamily Press} not getting processed correctly when having multiple of them on different bindings of the same action and receiving simultaneous input on all of them (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/new-input-system-stops-working-after-pressing-2-keyboard-buttons-at-the-same-time}{\texttt{ case 1364667}}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If, for example, you bind the A and S key on the same action, put a {\ttfamily Press} interaction on both, and then press both keys, interactions would get missed or got stuck.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Is\+Pressed}/{\ttfamily Was\+Pressed}/{\ttfamily Was\+Released} returning incorrect results when binding multiple buttons on the same action and pressing/releasing them simultaneously.
\item Improved performance of looking up actions by name.
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+controls} exhibiting bad performance when there were no controls bound to an action (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputaction-dot-controls-are-accessed-slower-when-the-gamepad-slash-controller-is-not-connected}{\texttt{ case 1347829}}).
\item Fixed interactions involving timeouts (such as {\ttfamily Hold\+Interaction}) performing erroneous delayed triggers on actions when input is composed of multiple controls (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-composites-hold-interaction-can-be-performed-when-no-keys-are-hold}{\texttt{ 1251231}}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item For example, if you bind {\ttfamily Shift+B} using a {\ttfamily One\+Modifier\+Composite} and put a {\ttfamily Hold\+Interaction} on the binding, then depending on the order in which the keys are pressed, you would sometimes see the action spuriously getting triggered when in fact no input was received.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed control schemes of bindings not getting updates when being pasted from one {\ttfamily .inputactions} asset into another (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-control-schemes-are-not-resolved-when-copying-bindings-between-inputactionassets}{\texttt{ case 1276106}}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item For example, if you copied a binding from an asset that had a "{}\+Gamepad"{} control scheme into an asset that had none, the resulting binding would be unusable.
\item All associations with control schemes that do not exist in the target asset are now removed from bindings upon pasting.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Setup\+Extensions.\+Add\+Composite\+Binding} not setting name of composite.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1068}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+2.\+0\mbox{]} -\/ 2021-\/10-\/22}{\mbox{[}1.\+2.\+0\mbox{]} -\/ 2021-\/10-\/22}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1068}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1069}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1069}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item When exceptions occur in user code inside of Input \doxylink{namespace_system}{System} callbacks, the exception message is now printed {\bfseries{first}} and details about the callback second.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Previously a message similar to "{}\+Exception ... while executing \textquotesingle{}...\textquotesingle{} callbacks"{} was printed first and then followed by exception log. This was hiding the actual exception and created confusion.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1070}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1070}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a performance issue on entering/exiting playmode where HID device capabilities JSON could be parsed multiple times for a single device(\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-package-deserializing-json-multiple-times-when-entering-slash-exiting-playmode}{\texttt{ case 1362733}}).
\item Fixed a problem where explicitly switching to the already active control scheme and device set for Player\+Input would cancel event callbacks for no reason when the control scheme switch would have no practical effect. This fix detects and skips device unpairing and re-\/pairing if the switch is detected to not be a change to scheme or devices. (case 1342297)
\item Any unhandled exception in {\ttfamily Input\+Manager.\+On\+Update} failing latter updates with {\ttfamily Invalid\+Operation\+Exception\+: Already have an event buffer set! Was On\+Update() called recursively?}. Instead the system will try to handle the exception and recover into a working state.
\item Fixed an issue that broke the {\ttfamily Virtual\+Mouse\+Input} component in the editor (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/vitrualmouseinput-stickaction-doesnt-work}{\texttt{ case 1367553}}).
\item Fixed a problem where only using runtimes that are not XR supported causes a compile error. This fix adds back in {\ttfamily ENABLE\+\_\+\+VR} checks to prevent this case (case 1368300)
\item Fixed input action for Android gamepad\textquotesingle{}s right stick will be correctly invoked when only y axis is changing (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/android-input-system-right-analog-stick-tracking-is-erratic-when-using-a-gamepad-connected-to-an-android-device}{\texttt{ case 1308637}}).
\item Generic gamepad short display button names were incorrectly mapped on Switch ({\ttfamily A} instead of {\ttfamily B}, etc).
\item Fixed an issue where resetting an action via {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Reset()} while being in disabled state would prevent the action from being enabled again. (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/1370732/}{\texttt{ case 1370732}}).
\item Fixed "{}\+Default constructor not found for type Unity\+Engine.\+Input\+System.\+i\+OS.\+Low\+Level.\+i\+OSStep\+Counter"{} any other potential exceptions due to classes, methods, fields and properties being stripped when managed stripping setting set to medium or high (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/ios-new-input-system-iosstepcounter-crash-on-launch-with-managed-stripping}{\texttt{ case 1368761}}).
\item Fixed an issue where {\ttfamily Invalid\+Operation\+Exceptions} are thrown if an input for an action with multiple interactions is held while disconnecting the device(\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-errors-are-thrown-when-disconnecting-controller-while-holding-a-button-with-press-and-release-set-up-separately}{\texttt{ case 1354098}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily action.\+Read\+Value} and others returning invalid data when used from {\ttfamily Fixed\+Update} or early update when running in play mode in the editor (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/enter-key-is-not-registered-when-using-waspressedthisframe-with-input-system-1-dot-1-1}{\texttt{ case 1368559}} \href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-action-readvalue-always-returns-zero-when-called-from-fixedupdate}{\texttt{ case 1367556}} \href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/querying-inputs-before-preupdate-dot-newinputupdate-returns-invalid-data-when-running-in-play-mode-in-editor}{\texttt{ case 1372830}}).
\item Fixed current being {\ttfamily null} for sensors ({\ttfamily Accelerometer.\+current}, others) (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/accelerometer-not-working-when-using-input-system-1-dot-1-1}{\texttt{ case 1371204}}).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1071}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1071}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added support for PS5 Dual\+Sense controllers on Mac and Windows.
\item Improved the user experience when creating single vs multi-\/touch touchscreen bindings in the Input Action Asset editor by making both options visible in the input action dropdown menu. Now it\textquotesingle{}s not neccessary to be aware of the touch\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}/press path binding syntax (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputsystem-touchscreens-multi-touch-doesnt-work-when-using-a-custom-inputactionasset}{\texttt{ case 1357664}}).
\item Added support for the \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} Remote app.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{NOTE}}\+: This unfortunately requires a change in the \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} native runtime. We are in the process of rolling out the change to \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} versions. A public build that receives the change will automatically enable the functionality in the Input \doxylink{namespace_system}{System} package.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1072}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+1.\+1\mbox{]} -\/ 2021-\/09-\/03}{\mbox{[}1.\+1.\+1\mbox{]} -\/ 2021-\/09-\/03}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1072}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1073}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1073}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Invalid\+Cast\+Exception\+: Specified cast is not valid.} and {\ttfamily Invalid\+Operation\+Exception\+: Already have an event buffer set! Was On\+Update() called recursively?} when upgrading from 1.\+1.\+0-\/pre.\+5 or earlier. If you experience this issue you can also restart the editor to resolve it.
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+Device\+Change.\+Destroyed} not being available, now it\textquotesingle{}s correctly marked as obsolete instead.
\item Removed documentation around platform user account management of {\ttfamily Input\+User} which was ahead of actual backend support for the feature.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1074}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+1.\+0\mbox{]} -\/ 2021-\/08-\/27}{\mbox{[}1.\+1.\+0\mbox{]} -\/ 2021-\/08-\/27}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1074}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1075}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1075}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Modified the fix that landed in {\ttfamily 1.\+1-\/preview.\+3} for \doxylink{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_same_control_multiple_times_fix}{any given control being added to an action only once}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This caused a regression with some setups that, for example, bound the same control multiple times in a composite using processors to alter the value of the control.
\item Internally, a control is now again allowed to feed into the same action through more than one binding.
\item However, externally the control will be mentioned on the action\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+controls} list only once.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Adding {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} from code now installs {\ttfamily Default\+Input\+Actions}. This is equivalent to the default setup when adding the component in the editor (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-ugui-button-does-not-react-when-clicked}{\texttt{ case 1259306}}). 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ go\ =\ \textcolor{keyword}{new}\ GameObject();}
\DoxyCodeLine{go.AddComponent<EventSystem>();}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ uiModule\ =\ go.AddComponent<InputSystemUIInputModule>();}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ uiModule.actionsAsset\ now\ has\ a\ DefaultInputActions()\ asset\ assigned\ to\ it\ and\ the\ various}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ action\ references\ point\ to\ its\ actions.}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module.\+Unassign\+Actions} has been added to remove all actions from the module en bloc. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{uiModule.UnassignActions();}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1076}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1076}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed an issue where mixing test cases based on {\ttfamily Input\+Test\+Fixture} (using mocked {\ttfamily Input\+System}) and regular test cases (using real {\ttfamily Input\+System}) would lead to static state leaking between test cases causing random failures and unexpected/undefined behavior (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/1329015}{\texttt{ case 1329015}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module.\+Assign\+Default\+Actions} not assigning {\ttfamily tracked\+Device\+Orientation} and {\ttfamily tracked\+Device\+Position}.
\item Fixed regression introduced by \doxylink{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_ui_multiple_scenes_fix}{previous change} where {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} would not disable actions correctly.
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+canceled} not getting triggered reliably for {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Type.\+Pass\+Through} actions when {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Reset\+Device} was called.
\item Fixed device resets (e.\+g. happening as part of focus changes) leading to only some actions bound to these devices getting cancelled instead of all of them.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1077}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+1.\+0-\/pre.\+6\mbox{]} -\/ 2021-\/08-\/23}{\mbox{[}1.\+1.\+0-\/pre.\+6\mbox{]} -\/ 2021-\/08-\/23}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1077}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1078}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1078}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed pairing devices to existing {\ttfamily Input\+User}s potentially corrupting list of paired devices from other {\ttfamily Input\+User}s (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-devices-are-reassigned-to-the-wrong-users-after-adding-a-new-device}{\texttt{ case 1327628}}).
\item Fixed duplication of control paths when viewing collections of {\ttfamily Input\+Control}s in the inspector.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fix contributed by \href{https://github.com/NibbleByte}{\texttt{ Nibble\+Byte}} in \href{https://github.com/Unity-Technologies/InputSystem/pull/1354}{\texttt{ 1354}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Stack\+Overflow\+Exception} caused by calling {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Update} from inside an input action callback such as {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+performed} (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/crash-when-adding-inputsystem-dot-update-to-inputsystem-command-handler-to-force-processing-an-event-and-sending-input}{\texttt{ case 1316000}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+Test\+Fixture} leaving all {\ttfamily .current} getters uninitialized after a test run (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputsystem-mouseeventhandler-breaks-when-running-multiple-playmode-tests}{\texttt{ case 1329015}}).
\item Fixed broken script references in Touch \doxylink{namespace_samples}{Samples} project (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-sample-projects-have-missing-script-references}{\texttt{ case 1190598}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Pointer\+Input} composite in {\ttfamily Touch\+Samples} project being registered only after scenes already loaded (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/mobile-input-system-custom-binding-broken-slash-not-registered-when-using-runtimeinitializeonloadmethod-and-loading-scene-directly}{\texttt{ case 1215048}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+Control\+Extensions.\+Enumerate\+Changed\+Controls} skipping over {\ttfamily left}, {\ttfamily right}, and {\ttfamily down} controls on PS4 controller\textquotesingle{}s dpad (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-left-right-and-down-directional-pad-buttons-do-not-switch-controls-over-to-controller}{\texttt{ case 1315107}}).
\item Fixed undo not working in {\ttfamily Input \doxylink{namespace_system}{System} Package} project settings pane (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputsystem-exception-thrown-continuously-when-undo-operation-is-performed-with-supported-devices-list-in-the-project-settings}{\texttt{ case 1291709}}).
\item Fixed incorrect indexing in {\ttfamily Input\+User.\+On\+Device\+Changed} that could result in incorrect pairing of devices or {\ttfamily Index\+Out\+Of\+Range\+Exception} being thrown when removing, adding or reconfiguring a device. Fix contribution by \href{https://github.com/ITR13}{\texttt{ Mikael Klages}} in \href{https://github.com/Unity-Technologies/InputSystem/pull/1359}{\texttt{ \#1359}}.
\item Fixed incorrect indexing when sorting magnitude based on score in {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Rebinding\+Extensions.\+Rebinding\+Operation} which could result in incorrect magnitudes for candidates. Contribution by \href{https://github.com/steinbitglis}{\texttt{ Fredrik Ludvigsen}} in \href{https://github.com/Unity-Technologies/InputSystem/pull/1348}{\texttt{ \#1348}}.
\item Fixed inconsistent ordering and execution when adding to or removing from the various callbacks in the API (such as {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+on\+Device\+Change} but also {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+started} etc.) during the execution of a callback (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputsystems-events-are-not-called-the-order-they-were-added-when-they-are-modified-in-the-middle-of-the-call-by-other-listener}{\texttt{ case 1322530}}.
\item Fixed inconsistent behavior of Web\+GL gamepad left/right stick. Up/\+Down controls were reverse of X/Y controls. (\href{https://fogbugz.unity3d.com/f/cases/1348959}{\texttt{ case 1348959}})
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Player\+Input\+Manager}s join action not triggering when using a referenced {\ttfamily Input\+Action} (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-player-input-managers-join-action-is-not-triggered-when-using-a-referenced-input-action}{\texttt{ case 1260625}}).
\item Fixed UI issue where pressing the wrong button was possible while quickly moving through a UI because the submit action fired on action press instead of action release (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-submit-action-is-called-on-release-rather-than-on-press-when-using-enter-key}{\texttt{ 1333563}}).
\item Fixed Invalid\+Operation\+Exception when opening a preset created from a .inputactions asset (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-properties-are-not-visible-and-invalidoperationexception-is-thrown-on-selecting-inputactionimporter-preset-asset}{\texttt{ case 1199544}}).
\item Fixed a problem arising when combining Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module and Play\+Input with Send\+Message or Broadcast\+Message callback behavior on the same game object or hierarchy which is an ambiguous input setup. This fix eliminates callbacks into Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module. Related to (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-ui-components-lags-when-using-input-system-ui-input-module-together-with-player-input-component}{\texttt{ 1343712}}).
\item Fixed inconsistent usage of {\ttfamily ENABLE\+\_\+\+PROFILER} define together with {\ttfamily Profiler.\+Begin\+Sample}/{\ttfamily Profiler.\+End\+Sample} by removing {\ttfamily ENABLE\+\_\+\+PROFILER} macro check because {\ttfamily Begin\+Sample}/{\ttfamily End\+Sample} are already conditional with {\ttfamily \mbox{[}Conditional("{}\+ENABLE\+\_\+\+PROFILER"{})\mbox{]}} (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inconsistent-enable-profiler-scripting-defines-in-inputmanager-dot-cs-when-using-profiler-dot-beginssample-and-profiler-dot-endsample}{\texttt{ case 1350139}}).
\item Remediated majority of performance issues with high frequency mice (\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}=1k\+Hz poll rates) in release mode by merging consecutive mouse move events together (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/many-input-events-when-using-1000hz-mouse}{\texttt{ case 1281266}}), see the events documentation for more information.
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+Event\+Trace} replays skipping over empty frames and thus causing playback to happen too fast.
\item Fixed {\ttfamily "{}\+Pointer should have exited all objects before being removed"{}} error when changing screen orientation on mobile.
\item Controls such as mouse positions are no longer reset when focus is lost.
\item Pressing a u\+GUI {\ttfamily Button} and then alt-\/tabbing away, letting go of the button, and then going back to the application will no longer trigger a button click.
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input.\+on\+Unpaired\+Device\+Activity} triggering from editor input.
\item Fixed \textquotesingle{}up\textquotesingle{} and \textquotesingle{}down\textquotesingle{} controls on {\ttfamily Web\+GLGamepad} left and right sticks not being clamped correctly.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1079}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1079}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed right-\/clicking in empty action map or action list not popping up context menu (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/cant-open-drop-down-menu-when-hovering-over-free-space-in-input-action}{\texttt{ case 1336426}}).
\item Fixed binding paths being misaligned in UI when switching to text mode editing (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-path-input-field-text-is-clipping-under-binding-in-the-properties-section}{\texttt{ case 1200107}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily "{}\+Exception\+: Style.\+Draw may not be called with GUIContent that is null."{}} error from {\ttfamily Player\+Input} inspector when having an action map with no actions (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/multiple-error-messages-are-thrown-when-trying-to-expand-the-event-list-of-an-input-actions-asset-that-has-an-empty-action-map}{\texttt{ case 1317735}}).
\item Fixed calling {\ttfamily Get\+Binding\+Display\+String()} on an {\ttfamily Input\+Action} with a composite binding leading to doubled up output (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/macos-input-system-getbindingdisplaystring-returns-empty-strings-for-some-mappings}{\texttt{ case 1321175}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Multi\+Tap\+Interaction} not respecting {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+multi\+Tap\+Delay\+Time} (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/multitapdelaytime-does-not-influence-maxtapspacing-in-input-action-assets}{\texttt{ case 1292754}}).
\item Fixed changing values in {\ttfamily Input \doxylink{namespace_system}{System} Package} project settings not affecting default values displayed in {\ttfamily .inputactions} editor window (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/multitapdelaytime-does-not-influence-maxtapspacing-in-input-action-assets}{\texttt{ case 1292754}}).
\item Fixed rebinding a part of a composite with {\ttfamily Rebinding\+Operation.\+With\+Target\+Binding} not also changing the type of control being looked for (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-performinteractiverebinding-method-doesnt-detect-button-input-when-rebinding-part-of-a-2d-vector-composite}{\texttt{ case 1272563}}).
\item \label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_axiscomposite-min-max-value-fix}%
\Hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_axiscomposite-min-max-value-fix}%

\end{DoxyItemize}Fixed {\ttfamily Axis\+Composite} not respecting {\ttfamily min\+Value} and {\ttfamily max\+Value} properties (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputsystem-1d-axis-composite-binding-will-return-a-incorrect-value-if-minvalue-and-maxvalue-is-not-1-and-1}{\texttt{ case 1335838}}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Argument\+Out\+Of\+Range\+Exception} caused by {\ttfamily Is\+Pointer\+Over\+Game\+Object} (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/mobile-argumentoutofrangeexception-is-thrown-when-calling-ispointerovergameobject}{\texttt{ case 1337354}}).
\item {\ttfamily Player\+Input} no longer logs an error message when it is set to {\ttfamily Invoke Unity\+Events} and can\textquotesingle{}t find an action in the given {\ttfamily .inputactions} asset (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/an-error-is-thrown-when-deleting-an-input-action-and-entering-play-mode}{\texttt{ case 1259577}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Hold\+Interaction} getting stuck when hold and release happens in same event (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-the-canceled-event-is-not-fired-when-clicking-a-button-for-a-precise-amount-of-time}{\texttt{ case 1346786}}).
\item Fixed adding an action in the {\ttfamily .inputactions} editor automatically duplicating interactions and processors from the first action in the map.
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Setup\+Extensions.\+Change\+Binding} when modifying binding from a different action than specified. Contribution by \href{https://github.com/steinbitglis}{\texttt{ Fredrik Ludvigsen}} in \href{https://github.com/Unity-Technologies/InputSystem/pull/1352}{\texttt{ \#1348}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1080}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1080}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+run\+Updates\+In\+Edit\+Mode} to enable processing of non-\/editor updates without entering playmode (only available for XR).
\item Added a new "{}\+UI vs Game Input"{} sample to the package. The sample can be installed from the \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} Package Manager UI in the editor.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The sample demonstrates how to deal with inputs that may both lead to UI actions as well as in-\/game actions.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added method {\ttfamily Set\+Motor\+Speeds\+And\+Light\+Bar\+Color} as a workaround for setting both the light bar and motor speeds simultaneously on a Dual\+Shock 4 controller (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/dualshock4-setlightbarcolor-and-setmotorspeeds-cannot-be-called-on-the-same-frame-using-input-system}{\texttt{ case 1271119}}).
\item Added the concept of "{}soft"{} and "{}hard"{} device resets.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item In general, resetting a device will reset its state to default values.
\item Individual controls can be marked as {\ttfamily dont\+Reset} to exclude them from resets. This makes the reset "{}soft"{} (default). 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ \ Perform\ a\ "{}soft"{}\ reset\ of\ the\ mouse.\ The\ mouse\ position\ will\ not\ be\ affected}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ but\ controls\ such\ as\ buttons\ will\ be\ reset.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{InputSystem.ResetDevice(Mouse.current);}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item A "{}hard"{} reset can be forced through the API. This also resets {\ttfamily dont\+Reset} controls. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Perform\ a\ "{}hard"{}\ reset\ of\ the\ mouse.\ The\ mouse\ position\ will\ also\ be\ reset\ to\ (0,0).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{InputSystem.ResetDevice(Mouse.current,\ alsoResetDontResetControls:\ true);}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item Resets will lead to {\ttfamily Input\+Action}s that are enabled and in-\/progress from controls that being reset, to be canceled. This will not perform actions even if they trigger on, for example, button release.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Device.\+can\+Run\+In\+Background} can now be force-\/set through layouts. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Force\ XInputWindows\ gamepads\ to\ not\ run\ in\ the\ background.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{InputSystem.RegisterLayoutOverride(\textcolor{stringliteral}{@"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}"{}name"{}"{}:\ "{}"{}XInputWindowsNoCanRunInBackground"{}"{},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}"{}extend"{}"{}:\ "{}"{}XInputWindows"{}"{},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}"{}runInBackground"{}"{}:\ "{}"{}off"{}"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}});}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item Improved performance of {\ttfamily Touchscreen} by merging consecutive touch move events together. See the events documentation for more information.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1081}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1081}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added a new {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+wants\+Initial\+State\+Check} property that allows toggling on initial state checks for {\ttfamily Button} and {\ttfamily Pass-\/\+Through} actions (implicitly enabled for {\ttfamily Value} actions).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This allows responding immediately to controls that are already actuated when the action is enabled.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added new API for more easily listening for event changes. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{InputSystem.onEvent}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ .ForDevice<Gamepad>()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ .Where(e\ =>\ e.HasButtonPress())}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ .CallOnce(e\ =>\ Debug.Log(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Button\ pressed!));}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item Added new API to easily listen for button presses on any device. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{InputSystem.onAnyButtonPress}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ .CallOnce(ctrl\ =>\ Debug.Log(\$\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Button\ '\{ctrl\}'\ pressed"{}}));}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This is a simple wrapper around the new API mentioned above.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1082}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1082}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Application focus handling behavior has been reworked.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item When {\ttfamily run\+In\+Background} is off, no action will be taken on focus loss. When focus comes back, all devices will receive a sync request. Those that don\textquotesingle{}t support it will see a "{}soft"{} reset.
\item When {\ttfamily run\+In\+Background} is on (which, when running in the editor, is considered to always be the case), a new setting {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+background\+Behavior} dictates how input is to be handled while the application does not have focus. The default setting of {\ttfamily Reset\+And\+Disable\+Non\+Background\+Devices} will soft-\/reset and disable all devices for which {\ttfamily Input\+Device.\+can\+Run\+In\+Background} is false. While in the background, devices that are flagged as {\ttfamily can\+Run\+In\+Background} will keep running as in the foreground.
\item In the editor, devices other than {\ttfamily Pointer} and {\ttfamily Keyboard} devices (i.\+e. anything not used to operate the editor UI) are now by default routing their input to the Game View regardless of focus. This also fixes the problem of gamepad sticks resetting to {\ttfamily (0,0)} on focus loss (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-gamepad-stick-values-are-cached-when-changing-editor-window-focus}{\texttt{ case 1222305}}).
\item A new setting {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+game\+View\+Focus} has been introduced to determine how Game View focused is handled in the editor with respect to input.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Editor\+: Removed \textquotesingle{}Lock Input to Game View\textquotesingle{} setting in the Input Debugger.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The setting has been replaced by the new \textquotesingle{}Game View Focus\textquotesingle{} project setting.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+default\+Button\+Press\+Point} is now clamped to a minimum value of {\ttfamily 0.\+0001} (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/onclick-not-working-when-in-player}{\texttt{ case 1349002}}).
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Device.\+On\+Configuration\+Changed} can now be overridden in derived classes.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} now defers removing pointers for touches by one frame.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This is to ensure that {\ttfamily Is\+Pointer\+Over\+Game\+Object} can meaningfully be queried for touches that have happened within the frame -- even if by the time the method is called, a touch has technically already ended (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-ispointerovergameobject-returns-false-when-used-with-a-tap-interaction}{\texttt{ case 1347048}}).
\item More precisely, this means that whereas before a {\ttfamily Pointer\+Exit} and {\ttfamily Pointer\+Up} was received in the same frame, a touch will now see a {\ttfamily Pointer\+Up} in the frame of release but only see a {\ttfamily Pointer\+Exit} in the subsequent frame.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Calling {\ttfamily Event\+System.\+Is\+Pointer\+Over\+Game\+Object()} from within {\ttfamily Input\+Action} callbacks (such as {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+performed}) will now result in a warning.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item UI updates {\itshape after} input and consumes input through {\ttfamily Input\+Action}s as they are processed. Thus, querying UI state from within {\ttfamily Input\+Action} callbacks will query outdated UI state.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Changed {\ttfamily Tracked\+Pose\+Driver} to use properties of type {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Property} rather than {\ttfamily Input\+Action} to allow more flexibility.
\item Changed quickstart documentation sample to use the Update method instead of Fixed\+Update to show a more correct usage of the {\ttfamily was\+Pressed\+This\+Frame} API.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1083}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+1.\+0-\/pre.\+5\mbox{]} -\/ 2021-\/05-\/11}{\mbox{[}1.\+1.\+0-\/pre.\+5\mbox{]} -\/ 2021-\/05-\/11}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1083}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixes a problem with the package\textquotesingle{}s manifest missing a dependency on the UI Elements module.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1084}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+1.\+0-\/pre.\+4\mbox{]} -\/ 2021-\/05-\/04}{\mbox{[}1.\+1.\+0-\/pre.\+4\mbox{]} -\/ 2021-\/05-\/04}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1084}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1085}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1085}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily Virtual\+Mouse\+Input} component is now part of the Input \doxylink{namespace_system}{System} assembly. It was previously packaged with the {\ttfamily Gamepad Mouse Cursor} sample.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The component has a different GUID from before, so existing setups that use the component from the sample are not broken. To use the built-\/in component you must explicitly switch over.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Test\+Fixture} no longer deletes the {\ttfamily Game\+Object}s in the current scene in its {\ttfamily Tear\+Down} (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-inputtestfixture-destroys-test-scene}{\texttt{ case 1286987}}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This was added for the sake of the Input \doxylink{namespace_system}{System}\textquotesingle{}s own tests but should not have been in the public fixture.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Generic {\ttfamily Gamepad} now has platform independent long button names. Previously it used different names if editor targeted PS4/\+Switch consoles (case 1321676).
\item When creating a new control scheme with a name {\ttfamily All Control Schemes}, {\ttfamily All Control Schemes1} will be created to avoid confusion with implicit {\ttfamily All Control Schemes} scheme (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/control-scheme-cannot-be-selected-when-it-is-named-all-control-schemes}{\texttt{ case 1217379}}).
\item Display names of keyboard buttons are now passed through {\ttfamily To\+Lower} and {\ttfamily To\+Title\+Case} to enforce consistent casing between different platforms and keyboard layouts (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/the-display-names-for-keyboard-keys-in-the-input-debugger-do-not-match-those-defined-in-input-system-package}{\texttt{ case 1254705}}).
\item Editor\+: All remaining {\ttfamily Input\+User} instances are now removed automatically when exiting play mode. This means that all devices are automatically unpaired.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item In essence, like {\ttfamily Input\+Action}, {\ttfamily Input\+User} is now considered a player-\/only feature.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Events queued {\bfseries{during}} event processing (i.\+e. {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Update()}) are now processed in the same frame. This eliminates the 1-\/frame lag previously incurred by simulated input.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Note that this does not extend to input queued {\bfseries{outside}} of event processing but in the same frame. For example, input queued by the UI (such as by {\ttfamily On\+Screen\+Button} and {\ttfamily On\+Screen\+Stick}) will still see a 1-\/frame lag as UI event processing happens later in the frame and outside of input event processing.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1086}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1086}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item When removing/unplugging a device, it will now also be removed from the device list of {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Map.\+devices} and {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Asset.\+devices}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ gamepad\ =\ InputSystem.AddDevice<Gamepad>();}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ actions\ =\ \textcolor{keyword}{new}\ MyGeneratedActions();}
\DoxyCodeLine{actions.devices\ =\ \textcolor{keyword}{new}[]\ \{\ gamepad\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{InputSystem.RemoveDevice(gamepad);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}actions.devices`\ is\ now\ an\ empty\ array.}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item Adding an action to a {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Map} that is part of an {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Asset} now requires all actions in the asset to be disabled (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/adding-actions-at-runtime-to-existing-map-from-asset-triggers-assertion-error}{\texttt{ case 1288335}}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This used to trigger an {\ttfamily Assert} at runtime but now properly throws an {\ttfamily Invalid\+Operation\+Exception}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1087}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1087}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed inputs in game view sometimes not working when running in the editor, as initial focus state could end up being incorrect.
\item Fixed bad performance in Input Debugger with high-\/frequency devices (e.\+g. 1+ KHz gaming mice). Before, high event volumes led to excessive refreshes of debugger data.
\item Fixed compile error on tv\+OS due to step counter support for i\+OS added in {\ttfamily 1.\+1.\+0-\/preview.\+3}.
\item Fixed PS4-\/ and PS3-\/specific {\ttfamily right\+Trigger\+Button} and {\ttfamily left\+Trigger\+Button} controls not being marked as synthetic and thus conflicting with {\ttfamily right\+Trigger} and {\ttfamily left\+Trigger} input (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-when-binding-gamepad-controls-triggerbutton-gets-bound-instead-of-triggeraxis}{\texttt{ case 1293734}}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This manifested itself, for example, when using interactive rebinding and seeing {\ttfamily right\+Trigger\+Button} getting picked instead of the expected {\ttfamily right\+Trigger} control.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed changes to usages of devices in remote player not being reflected in Input Debugger.
\item Fixed exceptions and incorrect values with HIDs using 32-\/bit fields (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputsystem-error-when-vjoy-is-installed}{\texttt{ case 1189859}}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This happened, for example, with v\+Joy installed.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+User} no longer sending {\ttfamily Input\+User\+Change.\+Controls\+Changed} when adding a new user after previously, all users were removed.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fix contributed by \href{https://github.com/SvenRH}{\texttt{ Sven Herrmann}} in \href{https://github.com/Unity-Technologies/InputSystem/pull/1292}{\texttt{ 1292}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Axis\+Deadzone\+Processor} min/max values not being settable to 0 in editor UI (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-input-system-axis-deadzone-minimum-value-fallsback-to-default-value-if-its-set-to-0}{\texttt{ case 1293744}}).
\item Fixed blurry icons in input debugger, asset editor, input settings (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputsystem-supported-device-list-dropdown-icons-present-under-project-settings-are-not-user-friendly}{\texttt{ case 1299595}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily click\+Count} not being incremented correctly by {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} for successive mouse clicks (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/eventdata-dot-clickcount-doesnt-increase-when-clicking-repeatedly-in-the-new-input-system}{\texttt{ case 1317239}}).
\item \label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_ui_multiple_scenes_fix}%

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Support for Device Simulator touchscreen input.
\item Enabled XR device support on Magic Leap (Lumin).
\item Added ability to force XR Support in a project by defining {\ttfamily UNITY\+\_\+\+INPUT\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+XR\+\_\+\+PLUGIN}.
\item Added a warning message to Player\+Input\+Manager editor when the attached input action asset won\textquotesingle{}t work with Join Players When Button Is Pressed behaviour due to missing control scheme device requirements (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-player-prefabs-are-not-instantiated-on-join-action-when-they-have-inputactionasset-assigned-to-them}{\texttt{ case 1265853}}).
\item Added support for \href{https://docs.unity3d.com/Manual/UIElements.html}{\texttt{ UI Toolkit}} with \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} 2021.\+1+.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item UITK is now supported as a UI solution in players. Input support for both \href{https://docs.unity3d.com/Manual/com.unity.ugui.html}{\texttt{ Unity UI}} and \href{https://docs.unity3d.com/Manual/UIElements.html}{\texttt{ UI Toolkit}} is based on the same {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} code path. More details in the manual.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} now has an {\ttfamily xr\+Tracking\+Origin} property. When assigned, this will transform all tracked device positions and rotations from it\textquotesingle{}s local space into \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity}\textquotesingle{}s world space (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/xr-sdk-tracked-device-raycaster-does-not-work-correctly-with-worldspace-canvas-when-xr-camera-is-offset-from-origin}{\texttt{ case 1308480}}).
\item Added {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module.\+Get\+Last\+Raycast\+Result}. This returns the most recent raycast result and can be used to draw ray visualizations or get information on the most recent UI object hit.
\item Added {\ttfamily Input\+State\+Block} support for {\ttfamily k\+Format\+SBit} when working with floats (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/hid-exceptions-are-thrown-when-launching-a-project-while-analog-keyboard-is-connected-to-the-machine}{\texttt{ case 1258003}}).
\item Added an API to parse control paths. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ parsed\ =\ InputControlPath.Parse(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}<XRController>\{LeftHand\}/trigger"{}}).ToArray();}
