\DoxyCodeLine{Debug.Log(parsed[1].name);\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Prints\ "{}trigger"{}.}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Can, for example, be used with {\ttfamily Input\+Binding.\+path}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added a new API-\/only setting in the form of {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+settings.\+max\+Event\+Bytes\+Per\+Update}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Puts an upper limit on the number of event bytes processed in a single update.
\item If exceeded, any additional event data will get thrown away and an error will be issued.
\item Set to 5MB by default.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added a new API-\/only setting called {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+settings.\+max\+Queued\+Events\+Per\+Update}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This limits the number of events that can be queued during event processing using the {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Queue\+Event} method. This guards against infinite loops in the case where an action callback queues an event that causes the same action callback to be called again.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module.\+Assign\+Default\+Actions} to assign default actions when creating ui module in runtime.
\item Added {\ttfamily UNITY\+\_\+\+INCLUDE\+\_\+\+TESTS} define constraints to our test assemblies, which is 2019.\+2+ equivalent to {\ttfamily "{}optional\+Unity\+References"{}\+: \mbox{[}"{}\+Test\+Assemblies"{}\mbox{]}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1090}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+1.\+0-\/preview.\+3\mbox{]} -\/ 2021-\/02-\/04}{\mbox{[}1.\+1.\+0-\/preview.\+3\mbox{]} -\/ 2021-\/02-\/04}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1090}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1091}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1091}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item An upper limit of 1024 controls per device and 1kb of memory state per device has been introduced.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This allows for certain optimizations.
\item Should the limits prove too tight, they can be raised in the future.
\item The most complex device we have at the moment ({\ttfamily Touchscreen}) has 242 controls and 616 bytes of state.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Touch\+Simulation} now {\bfseries{disables}} the {\ttfamily Pointer} devices it reads input from.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This is to address the problem of mouse input leading to {\bfseries{both}} mouse and touch input happening concurrently. Instead, enabling touch simulation will now effectively {\bfseries{replace}} mouse and pen input with touch input.
\item Devices such {\ttfamily Mouse} and {\ttfamily Pen} will remain in place but will not get updated. Events received for them will be consumed by {\ttfamily Touch\+Simulation}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Enabled XR device support on Switch.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1092}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1092}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed Right stick to use AXIS.\+Z and AXIS.\+RZ for Android gamepads.
\item Fixed triggers to always use Axis.\+Gas and Axis.\+Brake for Android gamepads.
\item Fixed precompiled layouts such as {\ttfamily Fast\+Keyboard} leading to build time regressions with il2cpp (case 1283676).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+Device.\+can\+Run\+In\+Background} not being correctly set for VR devices (thus not allowing them to receive input while the application is not focused).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+User.\+On\+Event} and {\ttfamily Rebinding\+Operation.\+On\+Event} exhibiting bad performance profiles and leading to multi-\/millisecond input update times (case 1253371).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item In our own measurements, {\ttfamily Input\+User.\+On\+Event} is \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}9 times faster than before and {\ttfamily Rebinding\+Operation.\+On\+Event} is \texorpdfstring{$\sim$}{\string~}2.5 times faster.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed PS4 controller not recognized on Mac when connected over Bluetooth (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-dualshock-4-zct1e-dualshock-2-v1-devices-are-not-fully-recognised-over-bluetooth}{\texttt{ case 1286449}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Enhanced\+Touch} leaking {\ttfamily Native\+Array} memory on domain reloads (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/new-input-system-simulated-touch-in-editor-doesnt-work}{\texttt{ case 1190150}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Touch\+Simulation} leading to {\ttfamily "{}\+Pointer should have exited all objects before being removed"{}} errors (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/new-input-system-simulated-touch-in-editor-doesnt-work}{\texttt{ case 1190150}}).
\item Fixed multi-\/touch not working with {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/android-onenddrag-not-being-called-when-there-are-at-least-2-touches-on-the-screen}{\texttt{ case 1271942}}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This also manifested itself when using On-\/\+Screen Controls and not being able to use multiple controls at the same time (for example, in the \href{https://github.com/UnityTechnologies/InputSystem_Warriors}{\texttt{ Warriors demo}}).
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed restart prompt after package installation not appearing on \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} 2020.\+2+ (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-after-package-install-the-update-slash-switch-and-restart-prompt-does-not-appear}{\texttt{ case 1292513}}).
\item Fixed action with multiple bindings getting stuck in {\ttfamily Performed} state when two or more controls are pressed at the same time (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-not-registering-multiple-inputs}{\texttt{ case 1295535}}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Regression introduced in 1.\+1-\/preview.\+2.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Touch.\+active\+Touches} having incorrect touch phases after calling {\ttfamily Enhanced\+Touch.\+Disable()} and then {\ttfamily Enhanced\+Touch.\+Enable()} (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/new-input-system-began-moved-and-ended-touch-phases-are-not-reported-when-a-second-scene-is-loaded}{\texttt{ case 1286865}}).
\item Fixed compile errors related to XR/\+AR on console platforms.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1093}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1093}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_same_control_multiple_times_fix}%
\Hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_same_control_multiple_times_fix}%

\end{DoxyItemize}Fixed actions not triggering correctly when multiple bindings on the same action were referencing the same control (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/1293808/}{\texttt{ case 1293808}}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Bindings will now "{}claim"{} controls during resolution. If several bindings {\bfseries{on the same action}} resolve to the same control, only the first such binding will successfully resolve to the control. Subsequent bindings will only resolve to controls not already referenced by other bindings on the action. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ action\ =\ \textcolor{keyword}{new}\ InputAction();}

\DoxyCodeLine{action.AddBinding(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}<Gamepad>/button*"{}});\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Will\ only\ receive\ buttonWest,\ buttonEast,\ and\ buttonNorth.}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item This also means that {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+controls} will now only contain any control at most once.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Fixed JSON serialization of action maps not preserving empty binding paths (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/cloning-actionmap-through-json-converts-empty-paths-to-null-which-is-not-allowed}{\texttt{ case 1231968}}).\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1094}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1094}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added Dual\+Shock4\+Gamepad\+Android and Xbox\+One\+Gamepad\+Android layout for Android
\item Added a new high-\/performance way to iterate over changed controls in an event.

\item This can be used, for example, to implement much more performant "{}any button pressed?"{} queries.

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added support for Step Counter sensors for i\+OS.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item You need to enable {\bfseries{Motion Usage}} under Input \doxylink{namespace_system}{System} settings before using the sensor. You can also manually add {\bfseries{Privacy -\/ Motion Usage Description}} to your application\textquotesingle{}s Info.\+plist file.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1095}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+1.\+0-\/preview.\+2\mbox{]} -\/ 2020-\/10-\/23}{\mbox{[}1.\+1.\+0-\/preview.\+2\mbox{]} -\/ 2020-\/10-\/23}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1095}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1096}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1096}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily submit} and the {\ttfamily cancel} actions of the UI input module now trigger on {\bfseries{release}} instead of press. This makes the behavior consistent with clicks triggering UI response on release rather than press.
\item Removed the old "{}\+Tanks"{} demo (previously available from the samples shipped with the package).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added a new and improved demo project, which you can download from the \href{https://github.com/UnityTechnologies/InputSystem_Warriors}{\texttt{ Input\+System\+\_\+\+Warriors}} Git\+Hub repository.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1097}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1097}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Actions of type {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Type.\+Button} now respect button press (and release) points.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Previously, button-\/type actions, when used without explicit "{}\+Press"{} interactions, would perform immediately when a bound control was actuated.
\item Now, a button-\/type action will behave the same as if a "{}\+Press"{} interaction is applied with "{}\+Trigger Behavior"{} set to "{}\+Press Only"{}.
\item This means that a button-\/type action will now perform (and perform {\bfseries{once}} only) when a control crosses the button press threshold defined in the global settings or, if present, locally on a {\ttfamily Button\+Control}. It will then stay performed and finally cancel only when the control falls back to or below the release threshold.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Read\+Value\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}T\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}()} now always returns {\ttfamily default\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}T\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} when the action is canceled.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This is to make it consistent with {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Callback\+Context.\+Read\+Value\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}T\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}()} which already returned {\ttfamily default\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}T\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} when the action was canceled.
\item In general, all APIs that read values will return default values when an action is in a phase other than {\ttfamily Started} or {\ttfamily Performed}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item If multiple actions in different action maps but in the same .inputactions asset have the same name, calling {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Asset.\+Find\+Action()} with just an action name will now return the first {\bfseries{enabled}} action. If none of the actions are enabled, it will return the first action with a matching name as before (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-action-can-only-be-triggered-by-one-of-the-action-maps-when-action-name-is-identical}{\texttt{ case 1207550}}). 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ map1\ =\ \textcolor{keyword}{new}\ InputActionMap(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}map1"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ map2\ =\ \textcolor{keyword}{new}\ InputActionMap(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}map2"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{map1.AddAction(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}actionWithSameName"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{map2.AddAction(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}actionWithSameName"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ asset\ =\ ScriptableObject.CreateInstance<InputActionAsset>();}
\DoxyCodeLine{asset.AddActionMap(map1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{asset.AddActionMap(map2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{map2[\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}actionWithSameName"{}}].Enable();}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ action\ =\ asset[\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}actionWithSameName"{}}];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Before:\ "{}map1/actionWithSameName"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Now:\ "{}map2/actionWithSameName"{}}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed player build causing {\ttfamily Project\+Settings.\+asset} to be checked out in Perforce (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/projectsettings-dot-asset-is-checked-out-in-perforce-when-building-a-project-with-the-input-system-package-installed}{\texttt{ case 1254502}}).
\item Fixed player build corrupting preloaded asset list in {\ttfamily Player\+Settings} if it was modified by another build processor.
\item Fixed remoting in Input Debugger not working for devices in the player that are created from generated layouts (such as XR devices).
\item Fixed potential {\ttfamily Null\+Reference\+Exception} in {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Property} when the {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Reference} is {\ttfamily null}.
\item Fixed "{}\+On-\/\+Screen Controls"{} sample still using {\ttfamily Standalone\+Input\+Module} and thus throwing {\ttfamily Invalid\+Operation\+Exception} when used with "{}\+Active Input Handling"{} set to "{}\+Input System Package (\+New)"{} (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-old-input-module-is-available-in-onscreencontrolssample-sample-scene-from-package}{\texttt{ case 1201866}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily On\+Screen\+Button} leaving button controls in pressed state when disabled in-\/between receiving {\ttfamily On\+Pointer\+Down} and {\ttfamily On\+Pointer\+Up}. Usually manifested itself by having to click the button twice next time it was enabled.
\item Fixed exiting out of play mode in the \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} Editor while a test run is in progress leading to the Input \doxylink{namespace_system}{System} permanently losing all its state until the editor is restarted (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/the-input-system-does-not-get-re-enabled-when-a-playmode-input-test-is-interrupted}{\texttt{ case 1251724}}).
\item Fixed max values for {\ttfamily Axis} and {\ttfamily Double} controls stored as multi-\/bit fields being off by one (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/value-equal-to-1-is-not-returned-by-the-input-system-when-reading-a-multi-bit-control}{\texttt{ case 1223436}}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fix contributed by \href{https://github.com/jamre}{\texttt{ jamre}} in \href{https://github.com/Unity-Technologies/InputSystem/pull/962}{\texttt{ 962}}. Thank you!
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed debug assert in {\ttfamily Input\+Device\+Tester} sample when simultaneously pressing two buttons on gamepad (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-runtime-errors-when-pressing-more-than-one-button-at-the-same-time}{\texttt{ case 1244988}}).
\item Fixed use of UI {\ttfamily Slider} causing drag thresholds to no longer work (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputsystem-drag-threshold-value-is-ignored-for-scroll-view-after-interacting-with-a-slider-slash-scroll-bar}{\texttt{ case 1275834}}).
\item Fixed layout lists in Input Debugger not updating when removing layouts.
\item Fixed device connects leading to different but similar device being reported as reconnected.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1099}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1099}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed Action with multiple bindings becoming unresponsive after a Hold interaction was performed (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-hold-interaction-makes-an-input-action-unresponsive-when-2-or-more-binding-are-attached-to-the-same-input-action}{\texttt{ case 1239551}}).

\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Trace.\+Action\+Event\+Ptr.\+Read\+Value\+As\+Object} leading to {\ttfamily Invalid\+Cast\+Exception} when trying to read values that came from composite bindings.
\item Fixed not being able to stack a {\ttfamily Multi\+Tap} on top of a {\ttfamily Tap} (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/multi-tap-and-tap-interactions-in-the-same-action-doesnt-work-properly}{\texttt{ case 1261462}}).
\item Fixed rebinds triggered by the Enter key causing stuck Enter key states (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-rebind-action-requires-two-inputs-slash-presses-when-using-the-enter-key}{\texttt{ case 1271591}}).

(\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/map-index-on-trigger-and-indexoutofrangeexception-errors-when-using-multiple-interactions-on-the-same-action}{\texttt{ case 1253034}}).
\item Fixed context menu in action editor not filtering out composites the same way that the {\ttfamily +} icon menu does. This led to, for example, a "{}2\+D Vector"{} composite being shown as an option for a button type action.
\item Fixed initial state checks for composite bindings failing if performed repeatedly. For example, doing a {\ttfamily Read\+Value\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Vector2\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} for a WASD binding would return an incorrect value after disabling the map twice while no input from the keyboard was received (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-cannot-read-vector2-values-after-inputactionset-has-been-disabled-and-enabled-twice}{\texttt{ case 1274977}}).
\item Fixed "{}\+Add Interaction"{} menu in action editor not filtering out interactions with incompatible value types (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/new-input-system-action-gets-called-only-once-when-using-mouse-press-interaction}{\texttt{ case 1272772}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Player\+Input} no longer auto-\/switching control schemes if {\ttfamily never\+Auto\+Switch\+Control\+Schemes} was toggled off and back on after the component was first enabled (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-auto-switch-locks-on-one-device-when-its-disabled-and-re-enabled-via-script}{\texttt{ case 1232039}}).
\item Fixed action map name being the same as .inputactions asset name leading to compile errors when {\ttfamily Generate C\# Class} is used; now leads to import error (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-user-can-name-inputaction-asset-and-action-map-the-same-creating-compilation-errors-on-generation}{\texttt{ case 1212052}}).
\item Fixed bindings not getting updated when binding by display name and there is no control with the given display name initially.

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1100}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1100}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added tv\+OS documentation entries in \textquotesingle{}Supported Input Devices\textquotesingle{} page.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1101}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1101}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added "{}release thresholds"{} for buttons.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Release points are now separated from press points by a percentage threshold.
\item The threshold is defined by {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+button\+Release\+Threshold}.
\item Thresholds are defined as percentages of press points. A release is thus defined as a button, after having reached a value of at least {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+default\+Button\+Press\+Point} (or whatever local press is used), falling back to a value equal to or less than {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+button\+Release\+Threshold} percent of the press point.
\item This is intended to solve the problem of buttons flickering around button press points.
\item The default threshold is set at 75\%, that is, buttons release at 3/4 of the press point.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added new methods to the {\ttfamily Input\+Action} class\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Is\+Pressed()}\+: Whether a bound control has crossed the press threshold and has not yet fallen back below the release threshold.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Was\+Pressed\+This\+Frame()}\+: Whether a bound control has crossed the press threshold this frame.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Was\+Released\+This\+Frame()}\+: Whether a bound control has fallen back below the release threshold this frame.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Was\+Performed\+This\+Frame()}\+: Whether the action was performed at any point during the current frame. Equivalent to {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+triggered}, which will be deprecated in the future.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Reset()}\+: Forcibly reset the action state. Cancels the action, if it is currently in progress.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Get\+Timeout\+Completion\+Percentage} to query the amount left to complete a currently ongoing interaction. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Let's\ say\ there's\ a\ hold\ interaction\ on\ a\ "{}warp"{}\ action.\ The\ user\ presses\ a\ button\ bound}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ to\ the\ action\ and\ then\ holds\ it.\ While\ the\ user\ holds\ the\ button,\ we\ want\ to\ know\ how\ much}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ longer\ the\ user\ will\ have\ to\ hold\ it\ so\ that\ we\ can\ display\ feedback\ in\ the\ UI.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ holdCompleted\ =\ playerInput.actions[\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}warp"{}}].GetTimeoutCompletionPercentage();}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item Added three new binding composite types\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily One\+Modifier\+Composite}\+: This is a generalization of {\ttfamily Button\+With\+One\+Modifier} (which is still available but now hidden from the UI) which also represents bindings such as "{}\+SHIFT+1"{} but now can be used to target bindings other than buttons (e.\+g. "{}\+SHIFT+delta"{}).
\item {\ttfamily Two\+Modifiers\+Composite}\+: This is a generalization of {\ttfamily Button\+With\+Two\+Modifiers} (which is still available but now hidden from the UI) which also represents bindings such as "{}\+SHIFT+\+CTRL+1"{} but now can be used to target bindings other than buttons (e.\+g. "{}\+SHIFT+\+CTRL+delta"{}).
\item {\ttfamily Vector3\+Composite}\+: Works the same way {\ttfamily Vector2\+Composite} does. Adds a {\ttfamily forward} and {\ttfamily backward} binding in addition to {\ttfamily up}, {\ttfamily down}, {\ttfamily left}, and {\ttfamily right}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1102}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+1.\+0-\/preview.\+1\mbox{]} -\/ 2020-\/08-\/20}{\mbox{[}1.\+1.\+0-\/preview.\+1\mbox{]} -\/ 2020-\/08-\/20}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1102}
\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}{\bfseries{The minimum version requirement for the Input \doxylink{namespace_system}{System} package has been moved up to 2019.\+4 LTS.}}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1103}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1103}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1104}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1104}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Auto-\/generated C\# files now have {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}auto-\/generated\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} headers so they get ignored by \doxylink{namespace_rider}{Rider} code analysis.
\item Auto-\/generated C\# classes are now {\ttfamily partial} so that they can be manually extended.
\item Deleting a composite binding with {\ttfamily action.\+Change\+Binding(0).Erase()} now also erases all the bindings that are part of the composite.
\item Trigger binding resolution from within action callbacks (e.\+g. {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+performed}) will now defer resolution until after the callback has completed.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This fixes crashes such as \href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/mecanim-crash-when-entering-or-exiting-play-mode-destroying-gameobjects}{\texttt{ case 1242406}} where disabling {\ttfamily Player\+Input} from within an action callback led to an action\textquotesingle{}s state being released while the action was still in a callback.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1105}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1105}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed input history on Android mono build by alligning memory of history records
\item Fixed no input being processed when running a {\ttfamily \mbox{[}Unity\+Test\mbox{]}} over several frames. Before, this required calling {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Update} manually.
\item Fixed clicking on help page button in \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} inspector for Input \doxylink{namespace_system}{System} components not going to relevant manual pages.
\item Fixed a bug that prevented Dual\+Shock controllers from working on tv\+OS. (case 1221223).
\item {\ttfamily Gravity\+Sensor}, {\ttfamily Linear\+Acceleration\+Sensor}, and {\ttfamily Attitude\+Sensor} not being initialized on i\+OS (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/1251382/}{\texttt{ case 1251382}}).
\item Fixed compilation issues with XR and VR references when building to platforms that do not have complete XR and VR implementations.
\item Fixed possible {\ttfamily Null\+Reference\+Exception}s on ARMs with controls that receive automatic memory offsets.
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Touch\+Control.\+tap\+Count} resetting to 0 when "{}\+Script Debugging"{} is enabled (case 1194636).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Touch.\+active\+Touches} not having a {\ttfamily Touch\+Phase.\+Began} entry for touches that moved in the same frame that they began in (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-mobile-enhancedtouch-screen-taps-start-with-moved-or-stationary-phase-instead-of-began}{\texttt{ case 1230656}}).
\item Fixed sequential taps causing touches to get stuck in {\ttfamily Touch.\+active\+Touches}.
\item Improved performance of {\ttfamily Touch.\+active\+Touches} (most notably, a lot of time was spent in endlessly repetitive safety checks).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Enhanced\+Touch} APIs not indicating that they need to be enabled with {\ttfamily Enhanced\+Touch\+Support.\+Enable()}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The APIs now throw {\ttfamily Invalid\+Operation\+Exception} when used without being enabled.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed memory corruption in {\ttfamily Input\+Event\+Trace.\+Allocate\+Event} (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-crash-with-various-stack-traces-when-using-inputactiontrace-dot-subscribetoall}{\texttt{ case 1262496}})
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Manifested itself, for example, as crashes when using {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Trace.\+Subscribe\+To\+All}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Axis\+Controls and Vector2\+Controls\textquotesingle{} X and Y subcontrols on XR devices now have a minimum range of -\/1 and a maximum range of 1. This means they can now properly respond to modifiers and interactions in the binding system.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1106}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1106}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed drag\&drop reordering actions while having one control scheme selected causing bindings from other control schemes to be lost (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-bindings-get-cleared-for-other-control-scheme-actions-when-reordering-an-action-in-a-specific-control-scheme}{\texttt{ case 122800}}).
\item Fixed stack overflow in {\ttfamily Player\+Input.\+Switch\+Current\+Action\+Map} when called from action callback (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputsystem-switchcurrentactionmap-causes-a-stackoverflow-when-called-by-each-pahse-of-an-action}{\texttt{ case 1232893}}).
\item Fixed control picker ending up empty when listing devices in "{}\+Supported Devices"{} (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/product/unity/issues/guid/1254150/}{\texttt{ case 1254150}}).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1107}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1107}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Device layouts can now be "{}precompiled"{} for speed. {\ttfamily Keyboard}, {\ttfamily Mouse}, and {\ttfamily Touchscreen} are now included as precompiled layouts greatly reducing instantiation time and GC heap cost for these devices. For {\ttfamily Touchscreen}, this results in a \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}20x speed-\/up for {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Add\+Device\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Touchscreen\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}()}.
\item Added Pose Control layout. The Pose Control is used on XR Devices and wraps tracking state, position, rotation, and velocity information.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1108}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1108}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Can now save binding overrides as JSON strings and restore them from such using the newly added {\ttfamily Save\+Binding\+Overrides\+As\+Json} and {\ttfamily Load\+Binding\+Overrides\+From\+Json} extension methods.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed compilation issues in {\ttfamily Tracked\+Device\+Raycaster} when disabling built-\/in XR module.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1111}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+0.\+0-\/preview.\+7\mbox{]} -\/ 2020-\/04-\/17}{\mbox{[}1.\+0.\+0-\/preview.\+7\mbox{]} -\/ 2020-\/04-\/17}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1111}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1112}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1112}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Virtual\+Mouse\+Input} not moving the software cursor when set to {\ttfamily Hardware\+Cursor\+Is\+Available} but not having a hardware cursor ()
\item Can now override built-\/in Android gamepad layouts. Previously, the input system would always choose its default defaults even after registering more specific layouts using {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Register\+Layout}.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Control\+Path.\+Try\+Get\+Control\+Layout} no longer throws {\ttfamily Not\+Implemented\+Exception} for {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Mouse\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}/scroll/x} and similar paths where the layout is modifying a control it inherited from its base layout (\href{https://forum.unity.com/threads/notimplementedexception-when-using-inputcontrolpath-trygetcontrollayout-on-mouse-controls.847129/}{\texttt{ thread}}).
\item Fixed compilation errors when disabling built-\/in VR and XR modules. (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/enable-input-system-symbol-is-not-being-updated-when-the-input-system-is-changed-in-player-settings/}{\texttt{ case 1214248}}).
\item Fixed compilation errors when disabling built-\/in Physics and Physics2D modules. (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputsystem-trackeddeviceraycaster-has-hard-references-on-both-physics-and-physics2d}{\texttt{ case 1191392}}).
\item No longer throws {\ttfamily Not\+Implemented\+Exception} when matching against a field of {\ttfamily Input\+Device\+Description.\+capabilities} when the value of the field used scientific notation.
\item No longer incorrectly matches fields of {\ttfamily Input\+Device\+Description.\+capabilities} by prefix only (i.\+e. previously it would find the field "{}foo"{} when actually looking for "{}foobar"{}).
\item Input device debugger window slowing editor to a crawl when opened on PS4 Dual\+Shock controller.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+User.\+Unpair\+Devices()} corrupting user device list.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1113}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1113}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Controls are now re-\/resolved after adding or removing bindings from actions (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-package-does-not-re-resolve-bindings-when-adding-a-new-binding-to-a-map-that-has-already-generated-its-state}{\texttt{ case 1218544}}).
\item Can now have spaces and special characters in action names when using {\ttfamily Player\+Input} with the {\ttfamily Send\+Messages} or {\ttfamily Broadcast\+Messages} behavior. Previously, an incorrect method name was generated (fix contributed by \href{https://github.com/BHSPitMonkey}{\texttt{ BHSPit\+Monkey}} in \href{https://github.com/Unity-Technologies/InputSystem/pull/1022}{\texttt{ \#1022}}; \href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/player-input-send-messages-wont-trigger-when-input-action-name-contains-spaces}{\texttt{ case 1214519}}).
\item Adding a new action now sets {\ttfamily expected\+Control\+Type} to {\ttfamily Button} as expected (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-default-value-of-expectedcontroltype-is-not-being-set-when-creating-a-new-action}{\texttt{ case 1221015}}).
\item \doxylink{class_player}{Player} joins with {\ttfamily Player\+Input\+Manager} from button presses no longer fail if there are multiple devices of the same type present and the join was not on the first gamepad (\href{https://fogbugz.unity3d.com/f/cases/1226920/}{\texttt{ case 226920}}).
\item {\ttfamily Player\+Input\+Editor} no longer leads to the player\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Asset} mistakenly getting replaced with a clone when the inspector is open on a {\ttfamily Player\+Input} component (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/action-map-gets-lost-on-play-when-prefab-is-highlighted-in-inspector}{\texttt{ case 1228636}}).
\item The control picker in the .inputactions editor will no longer incorrectly filter out layouts such as {\ttfamily Xbox One Gamepad (on XB1)} when using them in control schemes. Also, it will no longer filter out controls from base layouts (such as {\ttfamily Gamepad}) (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/impossible-to-choose-gamepad-as-binding-path-when-control-scheme-is-set-as-xboxone-scheme}{\texttt{ case 1219415}}).
\item {\ttfamily Rebind\+Operation}s will no longer pick controls right away that are already actuated above the magnitude threshold when the operation starts. Instead, these controls will have to change their actuation from their initial level such that they cross the magnitude threshold configured in the operation (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/unnecessary-slash-unwanted-binding-candidates-are-found-when-detecting-and-changing-an-input-value-of-an-input-device}{\texttt{ case 1215784}}).
\item Newly added actions and action maps are now scrolled to when there are more items than fit into view. Previously newly added item was appended but outside of the visible area.
\item Actions and bindings in the {\ttfamily .inputactions} editor are no longer force-\/expanded on every domain reload and whenever a new action or binding is added.
\item The importer for {\ttfamily .inputactions} assets will now check out from version control the generated .cs file when overwriting it -- which only happens if the contents differ (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputsystem-editor-generated-c-number-file-is-not-checked-out-when-overwriting}{\texttt{ case 1222972}}).
\item The editor for {\ttfamily .inputactions} assets will now check out from version control the asset before saving it.
\item Drag-\/reordering action maps no longer throws "{}\+Should have drop target"{} asserts in the console (case \href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputsystem-reordering-of-actionmaps-in-input-action-window-fails-and-throws-should-have-drop-target-error}{\texttt{ 1229146}}).
\item Drag-\/reordering actions no longer changes action IDs of some of the existing actions (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-systems-action-ids-dont-stick-with-action-names-when-input-actions-are-reorganized}{\texttt{ case 1231233}}).
\item References to {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Reference} objects created by the importer for {\ttfamily .inputactions} files are no longer broken when the action referenced by the object is renamed (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputsystem-inputactionreference-loses-guid-when-its-action-is-moved-or-renamed-in-the-inputaction-asset}{\texttt{ case 1229145}}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{NOTE\+: This fix does not apply to existing {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Reference} instances.}} The problem was inherent in the internal file IDs generated for actions -- which were affected by action and map names. Thus, changing the name of an action or map would change the resulting file ID of the {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Reference}.~\newline
However, changing file IDs will break any existing reference to the object. Thus we had to preserve the existing {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Reference} objects under their original file ID. We hide them in the Project Browser, however. The ones that are visible now have the new, fixed file IDs.~\newline
To switch existing {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Reference} properties to the new file IDs, simply replace them with the newly created {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Reference}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
