\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Device.\+all} has been deprecated due to the confusion it creates with other getters like {\ttfamily Gamepad.\+all}. Use {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+devices} instead (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/joystick-dot-all-lists-more-than-just-joysticks}{\texttt{ case 1231216}}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item In the same vein, we added a new {\ttfamily Joystick.\+all} getter that works the same as {\ttfamily Gamepad.\+all}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Changed UI Package to be optional dependency. Removing the package will now disable all UI relevant Input code.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1115}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+0.\+0-\/preview.\+6\mbox{]} -\/ 2020-\/03-\/06}{\mbox{[}1.\+0.\+0-\/preview.\+6\mbox{]} -\/ 2020-\/03-\/06}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1115}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1116}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1116}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module.\+tracked\+Device\+Select} has been removed. Use {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module.\+left\+Click} instead.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module.\+repeat\+Delay} has been renamed to {\ttfamily move\+Repeat\+Delay} and {\ttfamily repeat\+Rate} has been renamed to {\ttfamily move\+Repeat\+Rate}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1117}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1117}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed CS0109 warning being generated during player build due to use of {\ttfamily new} with the {\ttfamily Player\+Input.\+camera property} (case 1174688).
\item Fixed a number of issues in {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed GC heap garbage when click-\/dragging.
\item Fixed number of pointer states growing indefinitely if OS did not reuse touch IDs.
\item Fixed {\ttfamily last\+Press} on {\ttfamily Pointer\+Event\+Data} getting lost.
\item Fixed button press-\/and-\/release happening in same frame resulting in no UI input.
\item Fixed clicks initiated from non-\/pointer devices resulting in pointer inputs with {\ttfamily (0,0)} positions.
\item Fixed huge screen deltas on pointer events from tracked devices.
\item Fixed touch input not sending pointer exit events (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-onpointerexit-does-not-work}{\texttt{ case 1213550}}).
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Tracked\+Device\+Raycaster} not setting {\ttfamily screen\+Position} in {\ttfamily Raycast\+Result}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1118}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1118}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Mixing the enabling\&disabling of single actions (as, for example, performed by {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module}) with enabling\&disabling of entire action maps (as, for example, performed by {\ttfamily Player\+Input}) no longer leaves to unresponsive input and {\ttfamily "{}should not reach here"{}} assertions (\href{https://forum.unity.com/threads/error-while-switching-between-action-maps.825204/}{\texttt{ forum thread}}).
\item Leaving play mode no longer leaves state change monitors lingering around from enabled actions.
\item Enabling action maps with bindings that do not refer to an existing action in the map no longer leads to asserts and exceptions when input on the bindings is received (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-input-actions-cause-exceptions-and-should-not-get-here-errors-to-appear-after-deleting-an-action-map}{\texttt{ case 1213085}}).
\item {\ttfamily Press\+Interaction} no longer misses the next button press if it gets reset from within the {\ttfamily performed} callback (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputsystem-problem-with-button-state-after-deactivating-and-reactivating-an-action-map}{\texttt{ case 1205285}}).
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Binding.\+Display\+String\+Options.\+Dont\+Include\+Interactions} is now properly respected.
\item Reading the value of a composite binding no longer causes processors from the last active part binding to be applied rather than the processors of the composite itself, if any (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-invert-processors-have-no-effect-on-the-inputaction-dot-callbackcontext-value}{\texttt{ case 1207082}}).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+on\+Action\+Change} getting invoked too many times on binding changes.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1119}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1119}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} now sends pointer events using a new {\ttfamily Extended\+Pointer\+Event\+Data} instead of using the base {\ttfamily Pointer\+Event\+Data} class. This surfaces additional input data in pointer events.
\item Added {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module.\+pointer\+Behavior} to allow dictating how the UI will resolve concurrent input from multiple pointers.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1120}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1120}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Callback\+Context.\+Read\+Value\+As\+Button}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1121}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+0.\+0-\/preview.\+5\mbox{]} -\/ 2020-\/02-\/14}{\mbox{[}1.\+0.\+0-\/preview.\+5\mbox{]} -\/ 2020-\/02-\/14}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1121}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1122}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1122}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item We\textquotesingle{}ve changed the rules that govern how action phases have to progress\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{This is a breaking change!}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The primary effect is additional callbacks getting triggered.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Before}}\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item There were no enforced rules about how an action would go through {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+started}, {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+performed}, and {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+canceled}. Which of the callbacks were triggered and in what order depended on a number of factors, the biggest influencer of which were the different interactions that could be applied to actions (like {\ttfamily Press} or {\ttfamily Hold}).
\item This made for unpredictable and frequently surprising results. In addition, it led to bugs where, for \href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-ui-becomes-unresponsive-after-the-first-ui-button-press}{\texttt{ example}}, adding a {\ttfamily Press} interaction to the {\ttfamily Click} action of {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} would cause the click state to get stuck because the click action would never cancel.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Now}}\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The system will now {\itshape always} trigger {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+started} first. If this is not done explicitly, it happens implicitly.
\item Likewise, the system will now {\itshape always} trigger {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+canceled} before going back to waiting state. Like with {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+started}, if this isn\textquotesingle{}t done explicitly, it will happen implicitly. This implies that {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+canceled} no longer signifies an action getting aborted because it stopped after it started but before it performed. It now simply means "{}the action has ended"{} whether it actually got performed or not.
\item In-\/between {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+started} and {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+canceled}, {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+performed} may be triggered arbitrary many times (including not at all).
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item While late in the cycle for 1.\+0, we\textquotesingle{}ve opted to make this change now in order to fix a range of bugs and problems we\textquotesingle{}ve observed that people encountered because of the previous behavior of the system.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Related to the change above, the behavior of {\ttfamily Press\+Interaction} has been tweaked and now is the following\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Press Only}\+: Starts and immediately performs when pressed, then stays performed and cancels when button is released.
\item {\ttfamily Release Only}\+: Starts when button is pressed and then performs and immediately cancels when the button is released.
\item {\ttfamily Press And Release}\+: Starts and immediately performs when button is pressed, then stays performed and performs again and immediately cancels when button is released.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Vector2\+Composite} now has a {\ttfamily mode} parameter which can be used to choose between {\ttfamily Digital\+Normalized} (the default), {\ttfamily Digital} (same as {\ttfamily Digital\+Normalized} but does not normalize the resulting vector), and {\ttfamily Analog} (uses float input values as is).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Vector2\+Composite.\+normalize} has been deprecated. Note that it will not work together with {\ttfamily Analog}. The parameter will be removed in the future.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1123}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1123}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item XR controllers and HMDs have proper display names in the UI again. This regressed in preview.\+4 such that all XR controllers were displayed as just "{}\+XR Controller"{} in the UI and all HMDs were displayed as "{}\+XR HMD"{}.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} no longer generates GC heap garbage every time mouse events are processed.
\item Fixed a bug where an internal array helper method was corrupting array contents leading to bugs in both {\ttfamily Input\+User} and {\ttfamily Touch}.
\item Fixed exception when saving changes to an Input Action asset and the parent directory has been renamed. (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-console-errors-appear-when-you-save-input-action-asset-after-changing-the-name-of-the-folder-containing-it}{\texttt{ case 1207527}})
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1124}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1124}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The regression in 1.\+0.\+0-\/preview.\+4 of {\ttfamily Player\+Input\+Manager} not joining players correctly if a scheme has more than one device requirement has been fixed.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This most notably manifested itself with keyboard+mouse control schemes.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Player\+Input\+Manager} will no longer join players when control schemes are used and none of the schemes produces a successful match based on the devices available for the join.
\item When no action map is selected in action editor, plus icon to add an action is now disabled; formerly threw an exception when clicked (case 1199562).
\item Removing a callback from actions from the callback itself no longer throws {\ttfamily Argument\+Out\+Of\+Range\+Exception} (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-package-argumentoutofrangeexception-error-is-thrown-when-the-callback-is-removed-while-its-being-triggered}{\texttt{ case 1192972}}).
\item "{}\+Invalid user"{} {\ttfamily Argument\+Exception} when turning the same {\ttfamily Player\+Input} on and off (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-package-argumentexception-invalid-user-error-is-thrown-when-the-callback-disables-game-object-with-playerinput}{\texttt{ case 1198889}}).
\item The list of device requirements for a control scheme in the action editor no longer displays devices with their internal layout name rather than their external display name.
\item {\ttfamily Stack\+Overflow\+Exception} when {\ttfamily Invoke \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} Events} is selected in {\ttfamily Player\+Input} and it cannot find an action (\#1033).
\item {\ttfamily Hold\+Interaction} now stays performed after timer has expired and cancels only on release of the control (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/inputsystem-inputaction-dot-readvalue-returns-0-when-a-hold-action-is-performed-for-hold-time-amount-of-time}{\texttt{ case 1195498}}).
\item Foldouts in the various action UIs now properly toggle their expansion state when clicked in \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} 2019.\+3+ (\href{https://issuetracker.unity3d.com/issues/input-system-package-playerinput-component-events-menu-doesnt-expand-when-clicked-directly-on-the-arrow-icon}{\texttt{ case 1213781}}).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1125}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1125}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item We\textquotesingle{}ve added a new {\ttfamily Simple Multiplayer} sample which demonstrates a simple, bare-\/bones local multiplayer setup.
\item We\textquotesingle{}ve also added a {\ttfamily Gamepad Mouse Cursor} sample that shows how to drive a UI mouse cursor using the gamepad.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The sample contains a reusable {\ttfamily Virtual\+Mouse\+Input} component that does most of the work.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added a {\ttfamily Deselect On Background Click} option to {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module}. This allows toggling the behavior off where clicking the mouse and not hitting a {\ttfamily Game\+Object} will automatically clear the current selection -- which will break keyboard and gamepad navigation.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1126}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+0.\+0-\/preview.\+4\mbox{]} -\/ 2020-\/01-\/24}{\mbox{[}1.\+0.\+0-\/preview.\+4\mbox{]} -\/ 2020-\/01-\/24}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1126}
This release includes a number of Quality-\/of-\/\+Life improvements for a range of common problems that users have reported.\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1127}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1127}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item To aid in debugging issues, we\textquotesingle{}ve extended the system\textquotesingle{}s event tracing and replay functionality to allow persisting and replaying arbitrary input event streams.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Event\+Trace} now has APIs to persist the events to disk and to load them back in from previously persisted event streams. The same API can be used to persist in arbitrary C\# {\ttfamily Stream} instances, not just in file streams. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Write.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{myTrace.WriteTo(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}file.inputtrace"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Read.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{InputEventTrace.LoadFrom(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}file.inputtrace"{}});}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item {\ttfamily Input\+Event\+Trace} now has built-\/in replay functionality. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{myTrace.Replay().PlayAllFramesOneByOne();}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The event trace in device windows of the Input Debugger has been extended with controls to save and load traces.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item We\textquotesingle{}ve added a new {\ttfamily Input\+Recording} sample which has a reusable {\ttfamily Mono\+Behaviour} component that can be used to capture and replay device activity.
\item {\ttfamily Keyboard} now has a {\ttfamily Find\+Key\+On\+Current\+Keyboard\+Layout} method to look up key controls by their display names.
\item Keyboards now have synthetic controls that combine left and right variants of modifier keys.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This means that you can bind to just "{}shift"{} now, for example, instead of having to bind to both "{}left shift"{} and "{}right shift"{}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{new}\ InputAction(binding:\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}<Keyboard>/shift"{}});}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The controls are also available as properties on {\ttfamily Keyboard}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (Keyboard.current.shiftKey.isPressed)\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ ...\ */};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Is\ equivalent\ to:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (Keyboard.current.leftShiftKey.isPressed\ ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ Keyboard.current.rightShiftKey.isPressed)\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ ...\ */};}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1128}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1128}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Player\+Input} now has a new {\ttfamily Controls Changed} event/message which is triggered when the control setup of the player changes (e.\+g. when switching control schemes). 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{public}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ OnControlsChanged()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Update\ UI\ display\ hints,\ for\ example...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item We\textquotesingle{}ve added APIs to simplify turning bindings into strings suitable for display in UIs. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Takes\ things\ such\ as\ currently\ bound\ controls\ and\ active\ binding\ masks\ into\ account}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ can\ handle\ composites.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{action.GetBindingDisplayString();}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Related to this, custom binding composites can now be annotated with the new {\ttfamily Display\+String\+Format} attribute to control how composites as a whole are turned into display strings. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{[DisplayStringFormat(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\{button\}+\{stick\}"{}})]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{public}\ \textcolor{keyword}{class\ }MyComposite\ :\ InputBindingComposite<Vector2>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ [InputControl(layout\ =\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Button"{}})]\ \textcolor{keyword}{public}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ button;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ [InputControl(layout\ =\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Stick"{}})]\ \textcolor{keyword}{public}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ stick;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Rebinding\+Extension.\+Rebinding\+Operation} has a new configuration method {\ttfamily With\+Matching\+Events\+Being\+Suppressed} which allows suitable input events to automatically be swallowed while a rebind is ongoing. This greatly helps with not having something else respond to input while a rebind is in progress.
\item We\textquotesingle{}ve added two new samples\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Rebinding UI}}\+: Demonstrates how to create a rebinding screen using the Input \doxylink{namespace_system}{System}\textquotesingle{}s APIs. The sample also includes a reusable prefab you can use directly in your projects to quickly put rebinding screens together.
\item {\bfseries{In-\/\+Game Hints}}\+: Demonstrates how to show context-\/sensitive help that respects the current control scheme.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1129}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1129}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The logic for resetting devices on focus loss has changed somewhat\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item When focus is lost, all devices are forcibly reset to their default state. As before, a {\ttfamily Request\+Reset\+Command} for each device is also sent to the backend but regardless of whether the device responds or not, the input state for the device will be overwritten to default.
\item {\bfseries{Noisy controls are exempted from resets}}. The assumption here is that noisy controls most often represent sensor readings of some kind (e.\+g. tracking data) and snapping the values back to their default will usually
\item If {\ttfamily Application.\+run\+In\+Background} is {\ttfamily true}, all devices that return {\ttfamily true} from {\ttfamily Input\+Device.\+can\+Run\+In\+Background} are exempted from resets entirely. This, for example, allows XR devices to continue running regardless of focus change.
\item This fixes problems such as keyboard keys getting stuck when alt-\/tabbing between applications (case 1206199).
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Control\+Extensions.\+Get\+State\+Ptr\+From\+State\+Event} no longer throws {\ttfamily Invalid\+Operation\+Exception} when the state format for the event does not match that of the device. It simply returns {\ttfamily null} instead (same as when control is found in the event\textquotesingle{}s state).
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Event\+Trace} instances are no longer disposed automatically from their finalizer but {\bfseries{MUST}} be disposed of explicitly using {\ttfamily Dispose()}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This is to allow event traces to survive domain reloads. If they are disposed of automatically during finalizers, even if they survive the reload, the next GC will cause traces to be deallocated.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1130}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1130}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Rebinding\+Extensions.\+Perform\+Interactive\+Rebinding} has been greatly enhanced to apply a wide range of default configurations to the rebind. This greatly reduces the need to manually configure the resulting rebind. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Start\ a\ rebind\ with\ the\ default\ configuration.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{myAction.PerformInteractiveRebinding().Start();}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Pointer position input will be ignored by default.
\item If not a suitable binding target itself, {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Keyboard\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}/escape} will automatically be made to quit the rebind.
\item Events with control input not explicitly matching exclusions will now get suppressed. This prevents input actions from getting triggered while a rebind is in progress.
\item The expected control type is automatically adjusted if a part binding of a composite is targeted by the rebind (e.\+g. if the action expects a {\ttfamily Vector2} but the part binding expects a {\ttfamily Button}, the rebind switches automatically to {\ttfamily Button}).
\item If the targeted binding is part of a control scheme, controls will automatically be restricted to match the device requirements of the control scheme. For example, if the binding belongs to a "{}\+Keyboard\&\+Mouse"{} scheme that has {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Keyboard\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} and a {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Mouse\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} requirement, the rebind will ignore input on gamepads.
\item As before, you can always create a {\ttfamily Rebinding\+Operation} from scratch yourself or wipe/alter the configuration returned by {\ttfamily Perform\+Interactive\+Rebinding} however you see fit.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Control schemes can now handle ambiguity.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This means that, for example, you can now have one control scheme for generic gamepads and another control scheme specifically for PS4 controllers and the system will reliably pick the PS4 scheme when a PS4 controller is used and fall back to the generic gamepad scheme otherwise.
\item While this is exposed as a new {\ttfamily score} property on {\ttfamily Input\+Control\+Scheme.\+Match\+Result}, no code changes are necessary to take advantage of this feature.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Player\+Input.\+active} has been renamed to {\ttfamily Player\+Input.\+input\+Is\+Active} to avoid ambiguities with {\ttfamily Game\+Object} activation.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1131}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1131}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+User} in combination with touchscreens no longer throws {\ttfamily Invalid\+Operation\+Exception} complaining about incorrect state format.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item In a related change, {\ttfamily Input\+Control\+Extensions.\+Get\+State\+Ptr\+From\+State\+Event} now works with touch events, too.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Stack overflow in {\ttfamily Input\+Test\+Fixture.\+current\+Time} getter.
\item Input that occurs in-\/between pressing the play button and the game starting no longer leaks into the game (case 1191342).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This usually manifested itself as large accumulated mouse deltas leading to such effects as the camera immediately jerking around on game start.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Removing a device no longer has the potential of corrupting state change monitors (and thus actions getting triggered) from other devices.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This bug led to input being missed on a device once another device had been removed.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Tracked\+Device} layout is no longer incorrectly registered as {\ttfamily Tracked Device}.
\item Event traces in the input debugger are no longer lost on domain reloads.
\item {\ttfamily Index\+Out\+Of\+Range\+Exception} being thrown when looking up controls on XR devices.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1132}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1132}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Clicking the "{}\+Replace with Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module"{} button in the inspector when looking at {\ttfamily Standalone\+Input\+Module}, the resulting operation is now undoable and will properly dirty the scene.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1133}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+0.\+0-\/preview.\+3\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/11-\/14}{\mbox{[}1.\+0.\+0-\/preview.\+3\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/11-\/14}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1133}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1134}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1134}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed wrong event handlers getting removed when having three or more handlers on an event (case 1196143).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This was an bug in an internal data structure that impacted a number of code paths that were using the data structure.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Layout\+Not\+Found\+Exception} being thrown when {\ttfamily Input\+Control\+Path.\+To\+Human\+Readable\+String} referenced a layout that could not be found.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1135}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+0.\+0-\/preview.\+2\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/11-\/04}{\mbox{[}1.\+0.\+0-\/preview.\+2\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/11-\/04}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1135}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1136}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1136}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Automatic conversion of window coordinates in {\ttfamily Editor\+Window} code is now performed regardless of focus or the setting of {\ttfamily Lock Input to Game View} in the input debugger.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1137}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1137}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed touch taps triggering when they shouldn\textquotesingle{}t on Android.
\item Fixed custom devices registered from {\ttfamily \mbox{[}Initialize\+On\+Load\mbox{]}} code being lost on domain reload (case 1192379).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This happened when there were multiple pieces of {\ttfamily \mbox{[}Initialize\+On\+Load\mbox{]}} code that accessed the input system in the project and the {\ttfamily Register\+Layout} for the custom device happened to not be the first in sequence.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Open\+VR touchpad controls ({\ttfamily touchpad\+Clicked} \& {\ttfamily touchpad\+Pressed}) now report accurate data.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1138}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1138}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed missing keyboard bindings in {\ttfamily Default\+Input\+Actions.\+inputactions} for navigation in UI.
\item Fixed using C\# reserved names in .inputactions assets leading to compile errors in generated C\# classes (case 1189861).
\item Assigning a new {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Asset} to a {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} will no longer look up action names globally but rather only look for actions that are located in action maps with the same name.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Previously, if you e.\+g. switched from one asset where the {\ttfamily point} action was bound to {\ttfamily UI/\+Point} to an asset that had no {\ttfamily UI} action map but did have an action called {\ttfamily Point} somewhere else, it would erroneously pick the most likely unrelated {\ttfamily Point} action for use by the UI.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed missing custom editors for {\ttfamily Axis\+Deadzone\+Processor} and {\ttfamily Stick\+Deadzone\+Processor} that link {\ttfamily min} and {\ttfamily max} values to input settings.
\item Fixed actions ending up being disabled if switching to a control scheme that has no binding for the action (case 1187377).
\item Fixed part of composite not being bound leading to subsequent part bindings not being functional (case 1189867).
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Player\+Input} not pairing devices added after it was enabled when not having control schemes.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This problem would also show in the {\ttfamily Simple\+Demo} sample when having the {\ttfamily \doxylink{class_custom_device_usages}{Custom\+Device\+Usages}} sample installed as well. Gamepads would not get picked up in that case.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Argument\+Null\+Exception} when adding a device and a binding in an action map had an empty path (case 1187163).
\item Fixed bindings that are not associated with any control scheme not getting enabled with other control schemes as they should.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1139}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1139}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added a new {\ttfamily Editor\+Window Demo} sample that illustrates how to use the input system in editor UI code.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1140}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+0.\+0-\/preview.\+1\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/10-\/11}{\mbox{[}1.\+0.\+0-\/preview.\+1\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/10-\/11}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1140}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1141}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1141}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Generated action wrappers now won\textquotesingle{}t {\ttfamily Destroy} the generated Asset in a finalizer, but instead implement {\ttfamily IDisposable}.
\item Added back XR layouts (except for Magic Leap) that were removed for {\ttfamily 1.\+0-\/preview}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item We removed these layouts under the assumption that they would almost concurrently become available in the respective device-\/specific XR packages. However, this did not work out as expected and the gap here turned out to be more than what we anticipated.
\item To deal with this gap, we have moved the bulk of the XR layouts back and will transition things gradually as support in device-\/specific packages becomes publicly available.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1142}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1142}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug where the Input Settings Window might throw exceptions after assembly reload.
\item Correctly implemented {\ttfamily Is\+Pointer\+Over\+Game\+Object} method for {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module}.
\item Several bugs with layout overrides registered with ({\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Register\+Layout\+Overrides}).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item In {\ttfamily 1.\+0-\/preview}, layout overrides could lead to corruption of the layout state and would also not be handled correctly by the various editor UIs.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Selecting a layout in the input debugger no longer selects its first child item, too.
\item Fixed XR devices reporting noise as valid user input (should fix problem of control schemes involving VR devices always activating when using {\ttfamily Player\+Input}).
\item Fixed tap/swipe gesture detection in touch samples.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1143}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1143}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug where multiple composite bindings for the same controls but on different action maps would throw exceptions.
\item Fixed {\ttfamily any\+Key} not appearing in control picker for {\ttfamily Keyboard}.
\item The text on the "{}\+Listen"{} button is no longer clipped off on 2019.\+3.
\item Controls bound to actions through composites no longer show up as duplicates in the input debugger.
\item Fixed "{}\+Create Actions..."{} on {\ttfamily Player\+Input} creating an asset with an incorrect binding for taps on Touchscreens. \textbackslash{} {\bfseries{NOTE\+: If you have already created an .inputactions asset with this mechanism, update "{}tap \mbox{[}\+Touchscreen\mbox{]}"{} to "{}\+Primary Touch/\+Tap"{} to fix the problem manually.}}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Invoke CSharp Events} when selected in {\ttfamily Player\+Input} not triggering {\ttfamily Player\+Input.\+on\+Action\+Triggered}.
\item Fixed duplicating multiple items at the same time in the action editor duplicating them repeatedly.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1144}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1144}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Will now recognize Xbox One and PS4 controllers connected to i\+OS devices correctly as Xbox One and PS4 controllers.
\item Added a new sample called "{}\+Custom Device Usages"{} that shows how to use a layout override on {\ttfamily Gamepad} to allow distinguishing two gamepads in bindings based on which player the gamepad is assigned to.
\item Added abstract {\ttfamily Tracked\+Device} input device class as the basis for various kinds of tracked devices.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1145}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}1.\+0.\+0-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/09-\/20}{\mbox{[}1.\+0.\+0-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/09-\/20}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1145}

\item Fixed incorrect default state for axes on some controllers.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Callback\+Context.\+Read\+Value} throwing when invoked during device removal

\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1151}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1151}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Exceptions in scenes of {\ttfamily Visualizers} sample if respective device was not present on system (e.\+g. in {\ttfamily Pen\+Visualizer} if no pen was present in system).
\item Fixed exception in Input Action Asset Editor window when typing whitespace into the search field.
\item Fixed control scheme popup window in input action asset editor window showing in the correct screen position on windows.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1152}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1152}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Setting timeouts from {\ttfamily IInput\+Interaction.\+Process} not working as expected when processing happened in response to previous timeout expiring (\#714).
\item Pending timeouts on a device not being removed when device was removed.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1153}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1153}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Replaced {\ttfamily HIDSupport.\+should\+Create\+HID} event with a new {\ttfamily HIDSupport.\+supported\+HIDUsages} property, which takes an array of supported usages.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1154}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1154}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1155}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1155}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Player\+Input.\+never\+Auto\+Switch\+Control\+Schemes} to disable logic that automatically enables control scheme switching when there is only a single {\ttfamily Player\+Input} in the game.
\item Added {\ttfamily Player\+Input.\+Switch\+Control\+Scheme} to switch schemes manually.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1156}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}0.\+9.\+5-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/08-\/29}{\mbox{[}0.\+9.\+5-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/08-\/29}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1156}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1157}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1157}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Don\textquotesingle{}t pass events for null devices (for devices which have not been created) to {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+on\+Event} callbacks.
\item Will close debugger input state windows, when the state is no longer valid instead of throwing exceptions.
\item Fixed pointer coordinates in editor windows for non-\/mouse pointing devices.
\item Fixed using the input system in il2cpp when managed stripping level is set higher then "{}\+Low"{}.
\item Device debugger window will still show when reading from specific controls throws exceptions.
\item Offsets and sizes for elements on Linux joysticks are now computed correctly.
\item Joysticks now have a deadzone processor on the stick itself.
\item Up/down/left/right on sticks are now deadzoned just like X and Y on sticks are.
\item Removed toplevel {\ttfamily X} and {\ttfamily Y} controls on HIDs when there is a {\ttfamily Stick/X} and {\ttfamily Stick/Y} added for the device.
\item HID fallback can now deal with sticks that have X and Y controls of different sizes and sitting in non-\/contiguous locations in the HID input report.
\item Button 1 on HID joysticks will now correctly come out as the {\ttfamily trigger} control. Previously, the trigger control on the joystick was left pointing to random state.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1158}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1158}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Binding paths now show the same way in the action editor UI as they do in the control picker.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item For example, where before a binding to {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}XInput\+Controller\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}/button\+South} was shown as {\ttfamily right\+Shoulder \mbox{[}XInput\+Controller\mbox{]}}, the same binding will now show as {\ttfamily A \mbox{[}Xbox Controller\mbox{]}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item When deleting a control scheme, bindings are now updated. A dialog is presented that allows choosing between deleting the bindings or just unassigning them from the control scheme.
\item When renaming a control scheme, bindings are now updated. Previously the old name was in place on bindings.
\item Control scheme names can no longer be set to empty strings.
\item {\ttfamily Player\+Input.\+Instantiate} now correctly sets up a given control scheme, if specified.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item When passing a {\ttfamily control\+Scheme\+:} argument, the result used to be a correctly assigned control scheme at the {\ttfamily Input\+User} level but no restrictions being actually applied to the bindings, i.\+e. every single binding was active regardless of the specified control scheme.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Null\+Reference\+Exceptions during event processing from {\ttfamily Rebinding\+Operation}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1159}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1159}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+User.\+on\+Unpaired\+Device\+Used} now receives a 2nd argument which is the event that triggered the callback.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Also, the callback is now triggered {\bfseries{BEFORE}} the given event is processed rather than after the event has already been written to the device. This allows updating the pairing state of the system before input is processed.
\item In practice, this means that, for example, if the user switches from keyboard\&mouse to gamepad, the initial input that triggered the switch will get picked up right away.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Control\+Path.\+To\+Human\+Readable\+String} now takes display names from registered {\ttfamily Input\+Control\+Layout} instances into account.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This means that the method can now be used to generate strings to display in rebinding UIs.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Axis\+Control.\+clamp} is now an enum-\/valued property rather than a bool. Can now perform clamping {\itshape before} normalization.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1160}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1160}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item When switching devices/controls on actions, the system will no longer subsequently force an initial state check on {\bfseries{all}} actions. Instead, every time an action\textquotesingle{}s bindings get re-\/resolved, the system will simply cancel all on-\/going actions and then re-\/enable them the same way it would happen by manually calling {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Enable}.
\item Removed non-\/functional {\ttfamily Input\+Control\+Scheme.\+base\+Scheme} API and {\ttfamily based\+On} serialized property. This was never fully implemented.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1161}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1161}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Can right-\/click devices in Input Debugger (also those under "{}\+Unsupported"{}) and select "{}\+Copy Device Description"{} to copy the internal {\ttfamily Input\+Device\+Description} of the device in JSON format to the system clipboard.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This information is helpful for us to debug problems related to specific devices.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item If a device description has been copied to the clipboard, a new menu "{}\+Paste Device Description as Device"{} entry in the "{}\+Options"{} menu of the input debugger appears. This instantiates the device from the description as if it was reported locally by the \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} runtime.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1162}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}0.\+9.\+3-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/08-\/15}{\mbox{[}0.\+9.\+3-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/08-\/15}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1162}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1163}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1163}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily XInput\+Controller} and {\ttfamily Xbox\+One\+Gamepad} no longer have two extraneous, non-\/functional "{}menu"{} and "{}view"{} buttons.
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Input\+User.\+on\+Unpaired\+Device\+User} ignoring input on controls that do not support {\ttfamily Evaluate\+Magnitude}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This led to situations, for example, where {\ttfamily Player\+Input} would not initialize a control scheme switch from a {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Mouse\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}/delta} binding as the delta X and Y axes do not have min\&max limits and thus return -\/1 from {\ttfamily Evaluate\+Magnitude}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed available processor list not updated right away when changing the action type in the Input Action editor window.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1164}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1164}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Null\+Reference\+Exception} when the input debugger is open with actions being enabled.
\item When selecting a device to add to a control scheme, can now select devices with specific usages, too (e.\+g. "{}\+Left\+Hand"{} XRController).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1165}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1165}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Removed {\ttfamily timeslice\+Events} setting -\/ and made this tied to the update mode instead. We now always time slice when using fixed updates, and not when using dynamic updates.
\item When adding a composite, only ones compatible with the value type of the current action are shown. This will, for example, no longer display a {\ttfamily 2D Vector} composite as an option on a floating-\/point button action.
\item The {\ttfamily Input\+State.\+on\+Change} callback now receives a second argument which is the event (if any) that triggered the state change on the device.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1166}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1166}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} can now track multiple pointing devices separately, to allow multi-\/touch input -\/ required to allow control of multiple On-\/\+Scree controls at the same time with different fingers.
\item Two new composite bindings have been added.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Button\+With\+One\+Modifier} can be used to represent shortcut-\/like bindings such as "{}\+CTRL+1"{}.
\item {\ttfamily Button\+With\+Two\+Modifiers} can be used to represent shortcut-\/like bindings such as "{}\+CTRL+\+SHIFT+1"{}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1167}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}0.\+9.\+2-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/08-\/09}{\mbox{[}0.\+9.\+2-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/08-\/09}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1167}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1168}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1168}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item A {\ttfamily Rebinding\+Operation} will now fall back to the default path generation behavior if the callback provided to {\ttfamily On\+Generate\+Path} returns null.
\item Fixed the Input Action editor window throwing exceptions when trying to view action properties.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1169}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1169}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Player\+Input} will now copy overrides when creating duplicate actions.
\item It is now possible to use an empty binding path with a non empty override path.
\item It is now possible to use set an empty override path to disable a binding.
\item It is not possible to query the effectively used path of a binding using {\ttfamily effective\+Path}.
\item Actions embedded into Mono\+Behaviour components can now have their properties edited in the inspector. Previously there was no way to get to the properties in this workflow. There is a gear icon now on the action that will open the action properties.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1170}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1170}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1171}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1171}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added a new sample to the package called {\ttfamily Simple\+Demo}. You can install the sample from the package manager. See the \href{https://github.com/Unity-Technologies/InputSystem/Assets/Samples/SimpleDemo/README.md}{\texttt{ README.\+md}} file for details about the sample.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1172}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}0.\+9.\+1-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/08-\/08}{\mbox{[}0.\+9.\+1-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/08-\/08}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1172}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1173}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1173}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed GC heap garbage being caused by triggered by event processing.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This meant that every processing of input would trigger garbage being allocated on the managed heap. The culprit was a peculiarity in the C\# compiler which caused a struct in {\ttfamily Input\+Event\+Ptr.\+IsA} to be allocated on the heap.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item The bindings selection popup window will now show child controls matching the current action type even if the parent control does not match.
\item Fixed {\ttfamily duration} values reported for Hold and Press interactions.
\item Dual\+Shock 3 on mac\+OS\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed actions bound to the dpad control performing correctly.
\item Fixed non-\/present touchpad button control being triggered incorrectly.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed compile issues with switch classes on standalone Linux.
\item Leak of unmanaged memory in {\ttfamily Input\+Control\+List}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1174}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1174}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed actions not updating their set of controls when the usages of a device are changed.
\item Composite bindings with the default interaction will now correctly cancel when the composite is released, even if there are multiple composite bindings on the action.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1175}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1175}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Mouse\+State}, {\ttfamily Keyboard\+State}, and {\ttfamily Gamepad\+State} have been made public again.
\item {\ttfamily Player\+Input} and {\ttfamily Player\+Input\+Manager} have been moved from the {\ttfamily \doxylink{class_unity_engine_1_1_input_system_1_1_player_input}{Unity\+Engine.\+Input\+System.\+Player\+Input}} namespace to {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_input_system}{Unity\+Engine.\+Input\+System}}.
\item The signature of {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+on\+Event} has changed. The callback now takes a second argument which is the device the given event is sent to (null if there\textquotesingle{}s no corresponding {\ttfamily Input\+Device}). 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Before:}
\DoxyCodeLine{InputSystem.onEvent\ +=}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ eventPtr\ =>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ var\ device\ =\ InputSystem.GetDeviceById(eventPtr.deviceId);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //...}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Now:}
\DoxyCodeLine{InputSystem.onEvent\ +=}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ (eventPtr,\ device)\ =>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //...}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \};}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The signatures of {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+on\+Before\+Update} and {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+on\+After\+Update} have changed. The callbacks no longer receive an {\ttfamily Input\+Update\+Type} argument.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Use {\ttfamily Input\+State.\+current\+Update\+Type} in case you need to know the type of update being run.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Update\+Type} has been moved to the {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_input_system_1_1_low_level}{Unity\+Engine.\+Input\+System.\+Low\+Level}} namespace.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Update(\+Input\+Update\+Type)} has been removed from the public API.
\item The way input devices are built internally has been streamlined.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Device\+Builder} is now internal. It is no longer necessary to access it to look up child controls. Simply use {\ttfamily Input\+Control.\+Get\+Child\+Control} instead.
\item To build a device without adding it to the system, call the newly added {\ttfamily Input\+Device.\+Build} method. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{InputDevice.Build<Mouse>();}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Set\+Layout\+Variant} has been removed. Layout variants can no longer be set retroactively but must be decided on as part of device creation.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Register\+Control\+Processor} has been renamed to just {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Register\+Processor}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1176}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1176}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Read\+Value\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}TValue\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}()} is longer correlated to {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+triggered}. It simply returns the current value of a bound control or composite while the action is being interacted with.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Interaction\+Context.\+Performed\+And\+Go\+Back\+To\+Waiting} has been renamed to just {\ttfamily Input\+Interaction\+Context.\+Performed}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1177}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1177}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Individual composite part bindings can now no longer have interactions assigned to them as that never made any sense.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1178}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1178}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Devices can now have more than one usage.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Call {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Add\+Device\+Usage(device,usage)} to add additional usages to a device.
\item Call {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Remove\+Device\+Usage(device,usage)} to remove existing usages from a device.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Set\+Device\+Usage(device,usage)} still exists. It will clear all existing usages from the given device.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item A new {\ttfamily Visualizer\+Samples} sample that can be installed through the package manager.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Contains two components {\ttfamily Input\+Control\+Visualizer} and {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Visualizer} that help visualizing/debugging control/device and action activity through in-\/game overlays. A few sample scenes illustrate how to use them.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1179}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1179}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Read\+Value\+As\+Object} API.
\item Added {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+active\+Control} API.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1180}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}0.\+9.\+0-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/07-\/18}{\mbox{[}0.\+9.\+0-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/07-\/18}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1180}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1181}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1181}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Validate all parameters on public APIs.
\item Fixed an internal bug in {\ttfamily Inlined\+Array.\+Remove\+At\+By\+Moving\+Tail\+With\+Capacity}, which could cause data corruption.
\item Fixed Xbox controller support on mac\+OS il2cpp.
\item Fixed issue of Xbox gamepads on Windows desktop not being able to navigate left and down in a UI.
\item Allow using Input\+System package if the XR, VR or Physics modules are disabled for smaller builds.
\item Fixed documentation landing page and table of contents.
\item Fixed tracked devices assigning pointer ids for UI pointer events correctly.
\item Adjusted some UI Elements to fit the \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} 19.\+3 font.
\item Fixed Null\+Reference\+Exception being thrown when project changes.
\item Fixed duplicate devices showing in the "{}\+Supported Devices"{} popup when using a search filter.
\item Fixed an error when adding new bindings in the Input Actions editor window when a filter was applied.
\item Fixed scroll wheel handling in {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} not being smooth.
\item Fixed compile errors from Switch Pro controller code on Linux.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1182}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1182}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Callback\+Context.\+control} referencing the composite member control which was actually actuated for this trigger for composite bindings.
\item Generated C\# wrappers for .inputactions assets are no longer placed in Assets/\+Assets/ folder on Windows.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1183}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1183}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Touch support has been reworked and extended.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Touchscreen.\+touch\mbox{[}0..9\mbox{]}} are now bindable from the control picker.
\item {\ttfamily Touchscreen.\+primary\+Touch} is now a separate control which tracks the primary touch on the screen.
\item The controls {\ttfamily Touchscreen} inherits from {\ttfamily Pointer} (such as {\ttfamily position}, {\ttfamily phase}, and {\ttfamily delta}) are now tied to {\ttfamily Touchscreen.\+primary\+Touch} and allow for {\ttfamily Touchscreen} to function as a generic {\ttfamily Pointer} (like {\ttfamily Mouse} and {\ttfamily Pen}).
\item {\ttfamily Touchscreen.\+press} (renamed from {\ttfamily Touchscreen.\+button}) is now a working, synthetic button that is down whenever at least one finger is on the screen.
\item Recording of start time and start position has been added to touches.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Touch\+Control.\+start\+Position} gives the starting position of the touch.
\item {\ttfamily Touch\+Control.\+start\+Time} gives the starting time of the touch.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Tap detection has been added to {\ttfamily Touchscreen}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Tap time (i.\+e. time within which a press-\/and-\/release must be completed for a tap to register) corresponds to {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+default\+Tap\+Time}.
\item Tap release must happen within a certain radius of first contact. This is determined by a new setting {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+tap\+Radius}.
\item {\ttfamily Touch\+Control.\+tap} is a new button control that triggers then the touch is tapped. Note that this happens instantly when a touch ends. The button will go to 1 and {\bfseries{immediately}} go back to 0. This means that polling the button in {\ttfamily Update}, for example, will never trigger a tap. Either use actions to observe the button or use the {\ttfamily Touch} API from {\ttfamily Enhanced\+Touch} to poll taps.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Touchscreen.\+active\+Touches} has been removed. Use {\ttfamily Touch.\+active\+Touches} from the new enhanced touch API instead for more reliable touch tracking.
\item {\ttfamily Touchscreen.\+all\+Touch\+Controls} has been renamed to {\ttfamily Touchscreen.\+touches}.
\item A new {\ttfamily Enhanced\+Touch} plugin has been added which offers an enhanced {\ttfamily Touch} and {\ttfamily Finger} API to reliably track touches and fingers across updates. This obsoletes the need to manually track touch IDs and phases and gives access to individual touch history.
\item Touch can be simulated from mouse or pen input now. To enable simulation, call {\ttfamily Touch\+Simulation.\+Enable()} or put the {\ttfamily Touch\+Simulation} Mono\+Behaviour in your scene. Also, in the input debugger, you can now enable touch simulation from the "{}\+Options"{} dropdown.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Changing state has been decoupled from events. While input events are the primary means by which to trigger state changes, anyone can perform state changes manually now from anywhere. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{InputState.Change(gamepad.leftStick,\ new\ Vector2(123,\ 234));}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This change makes it possible to update state {\bfseries{from}} state and thus synthesize input data from other input coming in.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item A new API for recording state changes over time has been added. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ history\ =\ new\ InputStateHistory("{}<Gamepad>/leftStick"{});}
\DoxyCodeLine{history.StartRecording();}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//...}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{foreach\ (var\ record\ in\ history)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ Debug.Log(record);}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item Added support for generic joysticks on Web\+GL (which don\textquotesingle{}t use the standard gamepad mapping).
\item Added support for Dual\+Shock 3 gamepads on desktops.
\item Added support for Nintendo Switch Pro Controllers on desktops.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1184}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1184}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Actions now also have a {\bfseries{polling API}}!
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+triggered} is true if the action was performed in the current frame.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+Read\+Value\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}TValue\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}()} yields the last value that {\ttfamily started}, {\ttfamily performed}, or {\ttfamily cancelled} (whichever came last) was called with. If the action is disabled, returns {\ttfamily default(\+TValue)}. For {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Type.\+Button} type actions, returns {\ttfamily 1.\+0f} if {\ttfamily triggered==true} and {\ttfamily 0.\+0f} otherwise.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Generated C\# wrappers for .inputactions can now placed relative to the .inputactions file by specifying a path starting with \textquotesingle{}./\textquotesingle{} (e.\+g. {\ttfamily ./foo/bar.cs}).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1185}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1185}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{The system no longer supports processing input in {\bfseries{BOTH}} fixed and dynamic updates}}. Instead, a choice has to be made whether to process input before each {\ttfamily Fixed\+Update()} or before each {\ttfamily Update()}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Rationale\+: the existing code that supported having both updates receive input independently still had several holes and became increasingly complex and brittle. Our solution was based on not actually processing input twice but on channeling input concurrently into both the state of both updates. Together with the fact that specific inputs have to reset (and possibly accumulate) correctly with respect to their update time slices, this became increasingly hard to do right. This, together with the fact that we\textquotesingle{}ve come to increasingly question the value of this feature, led us to removing the capability while preserving the ability to determine where input is processed.
\item NOTE\+: Timeslicing is NOT affected by this. You can still switch to {\ttfamily Process\+Event\+In\+Fixed\+Updates} and get events timesliced to individual {\ttfamily Fixed\+Update} periods according to their timestamps.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+Update\+Mode.\+Process\+Events\+In\+Both\+Fixed\+And\+Dynamic\+Update} has been removed.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+Update\+Mode.\+Process\+Events\+In\+Dynamic\+Update\+Only} has been renamed to {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+Update\+Mode.\+Process\+Events\+In\+Dynamic\+Update} and is now the default.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+Update\+Mode.\+Process\+Events\+In\+Fixed\+Update\+Only} has been renamed to {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+Update\+Mode.\+Process\+Events\+In\+Fixed\+Update}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added icons for Player\+Input, Player\+Input\+Manager, Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module and Multiplayer\+Event\+System components.
\item Changed {\ttfamily Keyboard} IME properties ({\ttfamily ime\+Enabled}, {\ttfamily ime\+Cursor\+Position}) to methods ({\ttfamily Set\+IMEEnabled}, {\ttfamily Set\+IMECursor\+Position}).
\item Added getters to all {\ttfamily IInput\+Runtime} properties.
\item Replace some {\ttfamily Get\+Xxx} methods in our API with {\ttfamily xxx} properties.
\item {\ttfamily Pointer.\+phase} has been removed and {\ttfamily Pointer\+Phase} has been renamed to {\ttfamily Touch\+Phase}. Phases are now specific to touch. {\ttfamily Pointer\+Phase\+Control} has been renamed to {\ttfamily Touch\+Phase\+Control}.
\item {\ttfamily Pointer.\+button} has been renamed to {\ttfamily Pointer.\+press} and now is a control that indicates whether the pointer is in "{}press down"{} state.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item For mouse, corresponds to left button press.
\item For pen, corresponds to tip contact.
\item For touch, corresponds to primary touch contact (i.\+e. whether {\bfseries{any}} finger is down).
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item The state change monitor APIs ({\ttfamily IInput\+State\+Change\+Monitor} and friends) have been moved out of {\ttfamily Input\+System} into a new static class {\ttfamily Input\+State} in {\ttfamily Unity\+Engine.\+Experimental.\+Input.\+Low\+Level}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Rationale\+: These APIs are fairly low-\/level and not of general interest so having them out of {\ttfamily Input\+System} reduces the API surface visible to most users.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Device\+Change.\+State\+Changed} has been removed and is now a separate callback {\ttfamily Input\+State.\+on\+Change}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Rationale\+: The other {\ttfamily Input\+Device\+Change} notifications are low-\/frequency whereas {\ttfamily State\+Changed} is high-\/frequency. Putting them all on the same callback made adding a callback to {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+on\+Device\+Change} unnecessarily expensive.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily IInput\+State\+Callback\+Receiver} has been rewritten from scratch. Now has two simple methods {\ttfamily On\+Next\+Update} and {\ttfamily On\+Event}. If implemented by a device, the device now has completely control over changing its own state. Use the {\ttfamily Input\+State.\+Change} methods to affect state changes while trigger state change monitors (e.\+g. for actions) correctly.
\item Simplified handling of XR input in {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} by having only one set of actions for all XR devices.
\item We now use the same hierarchical device picker in the "{}\+Add Control Scheme"{} popup, which is already used in the "{}\+Input Settings"{} window.
\item Made all {\ttfamily IInput\+State\+Type\+Info} implementations internal, as these did not offer value to the user.
\item Made all {\ttfamily IInput\+Device\+Command\+Info} implementations internal, as these did not offer value to the user.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Read\+Write\+Array}, which was only used for making {\ttfamily Rebinding\+Operation.\+scores} editable, which did not add any value.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Primitive\+Value\+Or\+Array}, as non of it\textquotesingle{}s functionality over {\ttfamily Primitive\+Value} was implemented.
\item Made all {\ttfamily Input\+Processor} implementation internal, as access to these types is exposed only through text mode representations.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Curve\+Processor} as it was not implemented.
\item Renamed XInput\+Controller\+OSX to a more descriptive Xbox\+Gamepad\+Mac\+OS.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1186}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1186}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+continuous} has been removed. Running logic every frame regardless of input can easily be achieved in game code.
\item The way action behavior is configured has been simplified.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The previous roster of toggles has been replaced with two settings\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item {\ttfamily Action Type}\+: Determines the behavior of the action. Choices are {\ttfamily Value}, {\ttfamily Button}, and {\ttfamily Pass\+Through}.
\item {\ttfamily Control Type}\+: Determines the type of control (and implicitly the type of value) the action is looking for if the action is a {\ttfamily Value} or {\ttfamily Pass\+Through} action.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\item The previous {\ttfamily Initial State Check} toggle is now implicit in the action type now. {\ttfamily Value} actions perform an initial state check (i.\+e. trigger if their control is already actuated when the action is enabled). Other types of actions don\textquotesingle{}t.
\item The previous {\ttfamily Pass Through} toggle is now rolled into the action type.
\end{DoxyItemize}
