\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1187}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}0.\+2.\+10-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/05-\/17}{\mbox{[}0.\+2.\+10-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/05-\/17}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1187}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1188}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1188}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added a {\ttfamily Multiplayer\+Event\+System} class, which allows you use multiple UI event systems to control different parts of the UI by different players.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} now lets you specify an {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Asset} in the {\ttfamily actions\+Asset} property. If this is set, the inspector will populate all actions from this asset. If you have a {\ttfamily Player\+Input} component on the same game object, referencing the same {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Asset}, the {\ttfamily Player\+Input} component will keep the actions on the {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module} in synch, allowing easy setup of multiplayer UI systems.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1189}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1189}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Stick\+Control.\+x} and {\ttfamily Stick\+Control.\+y} are now deadzoned, i.\+e. have {\ttfamily Axis\+Deadzone} processors on them. This affects all gamepads and joysticks.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{NOTE\+:}} The deadzoning is {\bfseries{independent}} of the stick. Whereas the stack has a radial deadzones, {\ttfamily x} and {\ttfamily y} have linear deadzones. This means that {\ttfamily left\+Stick.\+Read\+Value().x} is {\bfseries{not}} necessary equal to {\ttfamily left\+Stick.\+x.\+Read\+Value()}.
\item This change also fixes the problem of noise from sticks not getting filtered out and causing devices such as the PS4 controller to constantly make itself {\ttfamily Gamepad.\+current}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Redesigned {\ttfamily UIAction\+Input\+Module}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added a button in the inspector to automatically assign actions from an input action asset based on commonly used action names.
\item Will now populate actions with useful defaults.
\item Removed {\ttfamily click\+Speed} property -\/ will use native click counts from the OS where available instead.
\item Removed {\ttfamily send\+Events\+When\+In\+Background} property.
\item Hiding {\ttfamily Touches} and {\ttfamily Tracked\+Devices} until we decide how to handle them.
\item Remove {\ttfamily move\+Deadzone} property as it is made redundant by the action\textquotesingle{}s dead zone.
\item Removed {\ttfamily UIAction\+Input\+Module\+Enabler} component, {\ttfamily UIAction\+Input\+Module} will now enable itself.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Changed default button press point to 0.\+5.
\item Changed all constants in public API to match \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} naming conventions ("{}\+Constant"{} instead of "{}k\+Constant"{}).
\item Changed namespace from {\ttfamily Unity\+Engine.\+Experimental.\+Input} to {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_input_system}{Unity\+Engine.\+Input\+System}}.
\item Generated wrapper code now has nicer formatting.
\item Renamed {\ttfamily UIAction\+Input\+Module} to {\ttfamily Input\+System\+UIInput\+Module}.
\item Nicer icons for {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Assets} and {\ttfamily Input\+Actions} and for {\ttfamily Button} and generic controls.
\item Change all public API using {\ttfamily Int\+Ptr} to use unsafe pointer types instead.
\item {\ttfamily Player\+Input} will no longer disable any actions not in the currently active action map when disabling input or switching action maps.
\item Change some public fields into properties.
\item Input \doxylink{namespace_system}{System} project settings are now called "{}\+Input System Package"{} in the project window instead of "{}\+Input (\+NEW)"{}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Plugins} from all namespaces.
\item Rename "{}\+Cancelled"{} -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} "{}\+Canceled"{} (US spelling) in all APIs.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1190}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1190}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Adding devices to "{}\+Supported Devices"{} in input preferences not allowing to select certain device types (like "{}\+Gamepad"{}).
\item Fixed scrolling in {\ttfamily UIAction\+Input\+Module}.
\item Fixed compiling the input system package in \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} 19.\+2 with ugui being moved to a package now.
\item In the Input \doxylink{namespace_system}{System} project settings window, you can no longer add a supported device twice.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1191}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1191}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Custom inspector for {\ttfamily Player\+Input} no longer adds duplicates of action events if {\ttfamily Invoke \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} Events} notification behavior is selected.
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Hold} interactions firing immediately before the duration has passed.
\item Fixed editing bindings or processors for {\ttfamily Input\+Action} fields in the inspector (Changes wouldn\textquotesingle{}t persist before).
\item Fixed exception message when calling {\ttfamily Callback\+Context.\+Read\+Value\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}TValue\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}()} for an action with a composite binding with {\ttfamily TValue} not matching the composite\textquotesingle{}s value type.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1192}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1192}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1193}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1193}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Player\+Input} can now handle {\ttfamily .inputactions} assets that have no control schemes.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Will pair {\bfseries{all}} devices mentioned by any of the bindings except if already paired to another player.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1194}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}0.\+2.\+8-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/04-\/23}{\mbox{[}0.\+2.\+8-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/04-\/23}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1194}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1195}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1195}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added a {\ttfamily click\+Count} control to the {\ttfamily Mouse} class, which specifies the click count for the last mouse click (to allow distinguishing between single-\/, double-\/ and multi-\/clicks).
\item Support for Bluetooth Xbox One controllers on mac\+OS.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1196}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1196}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item New API for changing bindings on actions 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Several\ variations\ exist\ that\ allow\ to\ look\ up\ bindings\ in\ various\ ways.}
\DoxyCodeLine{myAction.ChangeBindingWithPath("{}<Gamepad>/buttonSouth"{})}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ .WithPath("{}<Keyboard>/space"{});}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Can\ also\ replace\ the\ binding\ wholesale.}
\DoxyCodeLine{myAction.ChangeBindingWithPath("{}<Keyboard>/space"{})}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ .To(new\ InputBinding\ \{\ ...\ \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Can\ also\ remove\ bindings\ programmatically\ now.}
\DoxyCodeLine{myAction.ChangeBindingWithPath("{}<Keyboard>/space"{}).Erase();}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1197}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1197}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Joystick.\+axes} and {\ttfamily Joystick.\+buttons} have been removed.
\item Generated wrapper code for Input Action Assets are now self-\/contained, generating all the data from code and not needing a reference to the asset; {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Asset\+Reference} has been removed.
\item The option to generate interfaces on wrappers has been removed, instead we always do this now.
\item The option to generate events on wrappers has been removed, we felt that this no longer made sense.
\item Will now show default values in Input Action inspector if no custom values for file path, class name or namespace have been provided.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+run\+In\+Background} has been removed. This should now be supported or not on a per-\/device level. Most devices never supported it in the first place, so a global setting did not seem to be useful.
\item Several new {\ttfamily Sensor}-\/based classes have been added. Various existing Android sensor implementations are now based on them.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Control\+Layout\+Attribute} is no longer inherited.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Rationale\+: A class marked as a layout will usually be registered using {\ttfamily Register\+Layout}. A class derived from it will usually be registered the same way. Because of layout inheritance, properties applied to the base class through {\ttfamily Input\+Control\+Layout\+Attribute} will affect the subclass as intended. Not inheriting the attribute itself, however, now allows having properties such as {\ttfamily is\+Generic\+Type\+Of\+Device} which should not be inherited.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Removed {\ttfamily acceleration}, {\ttfamily orientation}, and {\ttfamily angular\+Velocity} controls from {\ttfamily Dual\+Shock\+Gamepad} base class.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item They are still on {\ttfamily Dual\+Shock\+Gamepad\+PS4}.
\item The reason is that ATM we do not yet support these controls other than on the PS4. The previous setup pretended that these controls work when in fact they don\textquotesingle{}t.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Marking a control as noisy now also marks all child controls as noisy.
\item The input system now defaults to ignoring any HID devices with usage types not known to map to game controllers. You can use {\ttfamily HIDSupport.\+supported\+Usages} to enable specific usage types.
\item In the Input Settings window, asset selection has now been moved to the "{}gear"{} popup menu. If no asset is created, we now automatically create one.
\item In the inspector for Input Settings assets, we now show a button to go to the Input Settings window, and a button to make the asset active if it isn\textquotesingle{}t.
\item \doxylink{namespace_tests}{Tests} are now no longer part of the com.\+unity.\+inputsystem package. The {\ttfamily Input\+Test\+Fixture} class still is for when you want to write input-\/related tests for your project. You can reference the {\ttfamily Unity.\+Input\+System.\+Test\+Fixture} assembly when you need to do that.
\item Implemented adding usages to and removing them from devices.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1198}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1198}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item A number of changes have been made to the control picker UI in the editor. \textbackslash{} 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The button to pick controls interactively (e.\+g. by pressing a button on a gamepad) has been moved inside the picker and renamed to "{}\+Listen"{}. It now works as a toggle that puts the picker into a special kind of \textquotesingle{}search\textquotesingle{} mode. While listening, suitable controls that are actuated will be listed in the picker and can then be picked from.
\item Controls are now displayed with their nice names (e.\+g. "{}\+Cross"{} instead of "{}button\+South"{} in the case of the PS4 controller).
\item Child controls are indented instead of listed in "{}parent/child"{} format.
\item The hierarchy of devices has been rearranged for clarity. The toplevel groups of "{}\+Specific Devices"{} and "{}\+Abstract Devices"{} are now merged into one hierarchy that progressively groups devices into more specific groups.
\item Controls now have icons displayed for them.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item There is new support for binding to keys on the keyboard by their generated character rather than by their location. \textbackslash{} 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item At the toplevel of the Keyboard device, you now have the choice of either binding by keyboard location or binding by generated/mapped character.
\item Binding by location shows differences between the local keyboard layout and the US reference layout.
\item The control path language has been extended to allow referencing controls by display name. {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Keyboard\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}/\#(a)} binds to the control on a {\ttfamily Keyboard} with the display name {\ttfamily a}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily continuous} flag is now ignored for {\ttfamily Press and Release} interactions, as it did not make sense.
\item Reacting to controls that are already actuated when an action is enabled is now an {\bfseries{optional}} behavior rather than the default behavior. This is a {\bfseries{breaking}} change.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Essentially, this change reverts back to the behavior before 0.\+2-\/preview.
\item To reenable the behavior, toggle "{}\+Initial State Check"{} on in the UI or set the {\ttfamily initial\+State\+Check} property in code. 
\item The reason for the change is that having the behavior on by default made certain setups hard to achieve. For example, if {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Keyboard\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}/escape} is used in one action map to toggle {\itshape into} the main menu and in another action map to toggle {\itshape out} of it, then the previous behavior would immediately exit out of the menu if {\ttfamily escape} was still pressed from going into the menu. \textbackslash{} We have come to believe that wanting to react to the current state of a control right away is the less often desirable behavior and so have made it optional with a separate toggle.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Processors and Interactions are now shown in a component-\/inspector-\/like fashion in the Input Action editor window, allowing you to see the properties of all items at once.
\item The various {\ttfamily Input\+Action.\+last\+Trigger\+XXX} APIs have been removed.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Rationale\+: They have very limited usefulness and if you need the information, it\textquotesingle{}s easy to set things up in order to keep track of it yourself. Also, we plan on having a polling API for actions in the future which is really what the {\ttfamily last\+Action\+XXX} APIs were trying to (imperfectly) solve.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Tap}, {\ttfamily Slow\+Tap}, and {\ttfamily Multi\+Tap} interactions now respect button press points.
\item {\ttfamily Tap}, {\ttfamily Slow\+Tap}, and {\ttfamily Multi\+Tap} interactions now have improved parameter editing UIs.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1199}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1199}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Input Settings configured in the editor are now transferred to the built player correctly.
\item Time slicing for fixed updates now works correctly, even when pausing or dropping frames.
\item Make sure we Disable any Input\+Action\+Asset when it is being destroyed. Otherwise, callbacks which were not cleaned up would could cause exceptions.
\item Dual\+Shock sensors on PS4 are now marked as noisy (\#494).
\item IL2\+CPP causing issues with XInput on windows and osx desktops.
\item Devices not being available yet in {\ttfamily Mono\+Behavior.\+Awake}, {\ttfamily Mono\+Behaviour.\+Start}, and {\ttfamily Mono\+Behaviour.\+On\+Enable} in player or when entering play mode in editor.
\item Fixed a bug where the event buffer used by {\ttfamily Input\+Event\+Trace} could get corrupted.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1200}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1200}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Actions and bindings disappearing when control schemes have spaces in their names.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Rebinding\+Exceptions.\+Rebind\+Operation} can now be reused as intended; used to stop working properly the first time a rebind completed or was cancelled.
\item Actions bound to multiple controls now trigger correctly when using {\ttfamily Press\+Interaction} set to {\ttfamily Release\+Only} (\#492).
\item {\ttfamily Player\+Input} no longer fails to find actions when using Unity\+Events (\#500).
\item The {\ttfamily "{}\{...\}"{}} format for referencing action maps and actions using GUIDs as strings has been obsoleted. It will still work but adding the extra braces is no longer necessary.
\item Drag\&dropping bindings between other bindings that came before them in the list no longer drops the items at a location one higher up in the list than intended.
\item Editing name of control scheme in editor not taking effect {\itshape except} if hitting enter key.
\item Saving no longer causes the selection of the current processor or interaction to be lost.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This was especially annoying when having "{}\+Auto-\/\+Save"{} on as it made editing parameters on interactions and processors very tedious.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item In locales that use decimal separators other than \textquotesingle{}.\textquotesingle{}, floating-\/point parameters on composites, interactions, and processors no longer lead to invalid serialized data being generated.
\item Fix choosing "{}\+Add Action"{} in action map context menu throwing an exception.
\item The input action asset editor window will no longer fail saving if the asset has been moved.
\item The input action asset editor window will now show the name of the asset being edited when asking for saving changes.
\item Clicking "{}\+Cancel"{} in the save changes dialog for the input action asset editor window will now cancel quitting the editor.
\item Fixed pasting or dragging a composite binding from one action into another.
\item In the action map editor window, switching from renaming an action to renaming an action map will no longer break the UI.
\item Fixed calling Enable/\+Disable from within action callbacks sometimes leading to corruption of state which would then lead to actions not getting triggered (\#472).
\item Fixed setting of "{}\+Auto-\/\+Save"{} toggle in action editor getting lost on domain reload.
\item Fixed blurry icons in editor for imported .inputactions assets and actions in them.
\item {\ttfamily Press} and {\ttfamily Release} interactions will now work correctly if they have multiple bound controls.
\item {\ttfamily Release} interactions will now invoke a {\ttfamily Started} callback when the control is pressed.
\item Made Vector2 composite actions respect the press points of button controls used to compose the value.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1201}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}0.\+2.\+6-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/03-\/20}{\mbox{[}0.\+2.\+6-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/03-\/20}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1201}
\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}NOTE\+: The UI code for editing actions has largely been rewritten. There may be regressions. \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}NOTE\+: The minimum version requirement for the new input system has been bumped to 2019.\+1\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1202}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1202}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Support gamepad vibration on Switch.
\item Added support for Joysticks on Linux.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1203}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1203}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added ability to change which part of a composite a binding that is part of the composite is assigned to.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Part bindings can now be freely duplicated or copy-\/pasted. This allows having multiple bindings for "{}up"{}, for example. Changing part assignments retroactively allows to freely edit the composite makeup.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Can now drag\&drop multiple items as well as drop items onto others (equivalent to cut\&paste). Holding ALT copies data instead of moving it.
\item Edits to control schemes are now undoable.
\item Control schemes are now sorted alphabetically.
\item Can now search by binding group (control scheme) or devices directly from search box.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily g\+:Gamepad} filters bindings to those in the "{}\+Gamepad"{} group.
\item {\ttfamily d\+:Gamepad} filters bindings to those from Gamepad-\/compatible devices.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1204}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1204}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The input debugger will no longer automatically show remote devices when the profiler is connected. Instead, use the new menu in debugger toolbar to connect to players or to enable/disable remote input debugging.
\item "{}\+Press and Release"{} interactions will now invoke the {\ttfamily performed} callback on both press and release (instead of invoking {\ttfamily performed} and {\ttfamily cancel}, which was inconsistent with other behaviors).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1205}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1205}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Bindings have GUIDs now like actions and maps already did. This allows to persistently and uniquely identify individual bindings.
\item Replaced UI overlay while rebinding interactively with cancellable progress bar. Interactive rebinding now cancels automatically after 4 seconds without suitable input.
\item Bindings that are not assigned to any control scheme are now visible when a particular control scheme is selected.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Bindings not assigned to any control scheme are active in {\itshape ALL} control schemes.
\item The change makes this visible in the UI now.
\item When a specific control scheme is selected, these bindings are affixed with {\ttfamily \{GLOBAL\}} for added visibility.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item When filtering by devices from a control scheme, the filtering now takes layout inheritance into account. So, a binding to a control on {\ttfamily Pointer} will now be shown when the filter is {\ttfamily Mouse}.
\item The public control picker API has been revised.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The simplest way to add control picker UI to a control path is to add an {\ttfamily Input\+Control\+Attribute} to the field. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ In\ the\ inspector,\ shows\ full\ UI\ to\ select\ a\ control\ interactively}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ (including\ interactive\ picking\ through\ device\ input).}
\DoxyCodeLine{[InputControl(layout\ =\ "{}Button"{})]}
\DoxyCodeLine{private\ string\ buttonControlPath;}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Processors of incompatible types will now be ignored instead of throwing an exception.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1206}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1206}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Remote connections in input debugger now remain connected across domain reloads.
\item Don\textquotesingle{}t incorrectly create non-\/functioning devices if a physical device implements multiple incompatible logical HID devices (such as the Mac\+Book keyboard/touch pad and touch bar).
\item Removed non-\/functioning sort triangles in event list in Input Debugger device windows.
\item Sort events in input debugger window by id rather then by timestamp.
\item Make parsing of float parameters support floats represented in "{}e"{}-\/notation and "{}\+Infinity"{}.
\item Input device icons in input debugger window now render in appropriate resolution on retina displays.
\item Fixed Xbox Controller on mac\+OS reporting negative values for the sticks when represented as dpad buttons.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+Update\+Mode.\+Process\+Events\+Manually} now correctly triggers updates when calling {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Update(Input\+Update\+Type.\+Manual)}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1207}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions}{Actions}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1207}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Pasting or duplicating an action in an action map asset will now assign a new and unique ID to the action.
\item "{}\+Add Action"{} button being active and triggering exceptions when no action map had been added yet.
\item Fixed assert when generating C\# class and make sure it gets imported correctly.
\item Generate directories as needed when generating C\# class, and allow path names without "{}\+Assets/"{} path prefix.
\item Allow binding dpad controls to actions of type "{}\+Vector2"{}.
\item Fixed old name of action appearing underneath rename overlay.
\item Fixed inspector UIs for on-\/screen controls throwing exceptions and being non-\/functional.
\item Fixed deleting multiple items at same time in action editor leading to wrong items being deleted.
\item Fixed copy-\/pasting actions not preserving action properties other than name.
\item Fixed memory corruptions coming from binding resolution of actions.
\item Input\+Action\+Asset\+References in Scriptable\+Objects will continue to work after domain reloads in the editor.
\item Fixed {\ttfamily start\+Time} and {\ttfamily duration} properties of action callbacks.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1208}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}0.\+2.\+1-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/03-\/11}{\mbox{[}0.\+2.\+1-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/03-\/11}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1208}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1209}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1209}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Native\+Update\+Callback API update to match \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} 2018.\+3.\+8f1
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1210}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}0.\+2.\+0-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/02-\/12}{\mbox{[}0.\+2.\+0-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2019-\/02-\/12}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1210}
This release contains a number of fairly significant changes. The focus has been on further improving the action system to make it easier to use as well as to make it work more reliably and predictably.

\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}NOTE\+: There are some breaking changes. Please see the "{}\+Changed"{} section below.\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1211}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1211}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Removed \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} 2018.\+2 support code.
\item Removed .NET 3.\+5 support code.
\item Started using C\# 7.
\item {\ttfamily IInput\+Control\+Processor\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}TValue\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} has been replaced with {\ttfamily Input\+Processor} and {\ttfamily Input\+Processor\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}TValue\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} base classes.
\item {\ttfamily IInput\+Binding\+Composite} has been replaced with an {\ttfamily Input\+Binding\+Composite} base class and the {\ttfamily IInput\+Binding\+Composite\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}TValue\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} interface has been merged with the {\ttfamily Input\+Binding\+Composite\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}TValue\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} class which had already existed.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+User.\+on\+Unpaired\+Device\+User} will now notify for each actuated control until the device is paired or there are no more actuated controls.
\item {\ttfamily Sensitivity\+Processor} has been removed.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The approach needs rethinking. What {\ttfamily Sensitivity\+Processor} did caused more problems than it solved.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item State monitors no longer have their timeouts removed automatically when they fire. This makes it possible to have a timeout that is removed only in response to a specific state change.
\item Events for devices that implement {\ttfamily IInput\+State\+Callbacks} (such as {\ttfamily Touchscreen}) are allowed to go back in time. Avoids the problem of having to order events between multiple fingers correctly or seeing events getting rejected.
\item {\ttfamily Pen\+State.\+Button} is now {\ttfamily Pen\+Button}.
\item Removed Touch\+Position\+Transform\+Processor, was used only by Android, the position transformation will occur in native backend in 2019.\+x
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1212}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Actions\+:}{Actions\+:}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1212}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Bindings that have no interactions on them will trigger differently now. {\bfseries{This is a breaking change}}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Previously, these bindings would trigger {\ttfamily performed} on every value change including when going back to their default value. This is why you would see two calls of {\ttfamily performed} with a button; one when the button was pressed, another when it was depressed.
\item Now, a binding without an interaction will trigger {\ttfamily started} and then {\ttfamily performed} when a bound control is actuated. Thereafter, the action will remain in {\ttfamily Started} phase. For as long as the control is actuated, every value change will trigger {\ttfamily performed} again. When the control stops being actuated, it will trigger {\ttfamily cancelled} and the action will remain in {\ttfamily Waiting} state.
\item Control actuation is defined as a control having a magnitude (see {\ttfamily Input\+Control.\+Evaluate\+Magnitude}) greater than zero. If a control does not support magnitudes (returns -\/1 from {\ttfamily Evaluate\+Magnitude}), then the control is considered actuated when it changes state away from its default state.
\item To restore the previous behavior, simply change code like 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{myAction.performed\ +=\ MyCallback;}

\end{DoxyCode}
 to 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{myAction.performed\ +=\ MyCallback;}
\DoxyCodeLine{myAction.cancelled\ +=\ MyCallback;}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item Alternatively, enable {\ttfamily pass\+Through} mode on an action. This effectively restores the previous default behavior of actions. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ new\ InputAction(binding:\ "{}<Gamepad>/leftTrigger"{})\ \{\ passThrough\ =\ true\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ @icode\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ As\ part\ of\ the\ aforementioned\ change,\ the\ following\ interactions\ have\ been\ removed\ as\ they\ are\ no\ longer\ relevant:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/\ \`{}StickInteraction`:\ Can\ simply\ be\ removed\ from\ bindings.\ The\ new\ default\ behavior\ obsoletes\ the\ need\ for\ what\ \`{}StickInteraction`\ did.\ Use\ \`{}started`\ to\ know\ then\ the\ stick\ starts\ being\ actuated,\ \`{}performed`\ to\ be\ updated\ on\ movements,\ and\ \`{}cancelled`\ to\ know\ when\ the\ stick\ goes\ back\ into\ rest\ position.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/\ \`{}PressAndReleaseInteraction`:\ Can\ simply\ be\ removed\ from\ bindings.\ The\ default\ behavior\ with\ no\ interaction\ encompasses\ press\ and\ release\ detection.\ Use\ \`{}started`\ to\ know\ then\ a\ button\ is\ pressed\ and\ \`{}cancelled`\ to\ know\ when\ it\ is\ released.\ To\ set\ a\ custom\ button\ press\ point,\ simply\ put\ an\ \`{}AxisDeadzoneProcessor`\ on\ the\ binding.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \`{}PressInteraction`\ has\ been\ completely\ rewritten.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/\ Trigger\ behavior\ can\ be\ set\ through\ \`{}behavior`\ parameter\ and\ now\ provides\ options\ for\ observing\ just\ presses\ (`PressOnly`),\ just\ releases\ (`ReleaseOnly`),\ or\ both\ presses\ and\ releases\ (`PressAndRelease`).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/\ Also,\ the\ interaction\ now\ operates\ on\ control\ actuation\ rather\ than\ reading\ out\ float\ values\ directly.\ This\ means\ that\ any\ control\ that\ supports\ magnitudes\ can\ be\ used.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/\ Also\ supports\ continuous\ mode\ now.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ If\ bound\ controls\ are\ already\ actuated\ when\ an\ action\ is\ enabled,\ the\ action\ will\ now\ trigger\ in\ the\ next\ input\ update\ as\ if\ the\ control\ had\ just\ been\ moved\ from\ non-\/actuated\ to\ actuated\ state.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/\ In\ other\ words,\ if\ e.g.\ you\ have\ a\ binding\ to\ the\ A\ button\ of\ the\ gamepad\ and\ the\ A\ button\ is\ already\ pressed\ when\ the\ action\ is\ first\ enabled,\ then\ the\ action\ associated\ with\ the\ A\ button\ will\ trigger\ as\ if\ the\ button\ had\ just\ been\ pressed.\ Previously,\ it\ required\ releasing\ and\ re-\/pressing\ the\ button\ first\ -\/-\/\ which,\ together\ with\ certain\ interactions,\ could\ lead\ to\ actions\ ending\ up\ in\ a\ confused\ state.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ When\ an\ action\ is\ disabled,\ it\ will\ now\ cancel\ all\ ongoing\ interactions,\ if\ any\ (i.e.\ you\ will\ see\ \`{}InputAction.cancelled`\ being\ called).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/\ Note\ that\ unlike\ the\ above-\/mentioned\ callbacks\ that\ happen\ when\ an\ action\ starts\ out\ with\ a\ control\ already\ actuated,\ the\ cancellation\ callbacks\ happen\ \_\_immediately\_\_\ rather\ than\ in\ the\ next\ input\ update.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ Actions\ that\ at\ runtime\ are\ bound\ to\ multiple\ controls\ will\ now\ perform\ *conflict\ resolution*,\ if\ necessary.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/\ This\ applies\ only\ if\ an\ action\ actually\ receives\ multiple\ concurrent\ actuations\ from\ controls.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/\ When\ ambiguity\ is\ detected,\ the\ greatest\ amount\ of\ actuation\ on\ any\ of\ the\ controls\ gets\ to\ drive\ the\ action.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/\ In\ practice,\ this\ means\ that\ as\ long\ as\ any\ of\ the\ controls\ bound\ to\ an\ action\ is\ actuated,\ the\ action\ will\ keep\ going.\ This\ resolves\ ambiguities\ when\ an\ action\ has\ primary\ and\ secondary\ bindings,\ for\ examples,\ or\ when\ an\ action\ is\ bound\ to\ multiple\ different\ devices\ at\ the\ same\ time.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/\ Composite\ bindings\ count\ as\ single\ actuations\ regardless\ of\ how\ many\ controls\ participate\ in\ the\ composite.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/\ This\ behavior\ \_\_can\ be\ bypassed\_\_\ by\ setting\ the\ action\ to\ be\ pass-\/through.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ Action\ editor\ now\ closes\ when\ asset\ is\ deleted.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/\ If\ there\ are\ unsaved\ changes,\ asks\ for\ confirmation\ first.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ Interactions\ and\ processors\ in\ the\ UI\ are\ now\ filtered\ based\ on\ the\ type\ of\ the\ action\ (if\ set)\ and\ sorted\ by\ name.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ Renamed\ "{}Axis"{}\ and\ "{}Dpad"{}\ composites\ to\ "{}1D\ Axis"{}\ and\ "{}2D\ Vector"{}\ composite.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/\ The\ old\ names\ can\ still\ be\ used\ and\ existing\ data\ will\ load\ as\ expected.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/\ \`{}DpadComposite`\ got\ renamed\ to\ \`{}Vector2Composite`;\ \`{}AxisComposite`\ is\ unchanged.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \`{}InputInteractionContext.controlHasDefaultValue`\ has\ been\ replaced\ with\ \`{}InputInteractionContext.ControlIsActuated()`.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \`{}InputActionChange.BindingsHaveChangedWhileEnabled`\ has\ been\ reworked\ and\ split\ in\ two:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ 1.\ \`{}InputActionChange.BoundControlsAboutToChange`:\ Bindings\ have\ been\ previously\ resolved\ but\ are\ about\ to\ be\ re-\/resolved.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ 2.\ \`{}InputActionChange.BoundControlsChanged`:\ Bindings\ have\ been\ resolved\ on\ one\ or\ more\ actions.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ Actions\ internally\ now\ allocate\ unmanaged\ memory.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/\ Disposing\ should\ be\ taken\ care\ of\ automatically\ (though\ you\ can\ manually\ \`{}Dispose`\ as\ well).\ If\ you\ see\ errors\ in\ the\ console\ log\ about\ unmanaged\ memory\ being\ leaked,\ please\ report\ the\ bug.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/\ All\ execution\ state\ except\ for\ C\#\ heap\ objects\ for\ processors,\ interactions,\ and\ composites\ has\ been\ collapsed\ into\ a\ single\ block\ of\ unmanaged\ memory.\ Actions\ should\ now\ be\ able\ to\ re-\/resolve\ efficiently\ without\ allocating\ additional\ GC\ memory.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\#\#\#\ Added}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \`{}PlayerInput`\ component\ which\ simplifies\ setting\ up\ individual\ player\ input\ actions\ and\ device\ pairings.\ \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ![PlayerInput](Documentation\string~/Images/PlayerInput.png)}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \`{}PlayerInputManager`\ component\ which\ simplifies\ player\ joining\ and\ split-\/screen\ setups.\ \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ![PlayerInput](Documentation\string~/Images/PlayerInputManager.png)}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \`{}InputDevice.all`\ (equivalent\ to\ \`{}InputSystem.devices`)}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \`{}InputControl.IsActuated()`\ can\ be\ used\ to\ determine\ whether\ control\ is\ currently\ actuated\ (defined\ as\ extension\ method\ in\ \`{}InputControlExtensions`).}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ Can\ now\ read\ control\ values\ from\ buffers\ as\ objects\ using\ \`{}InputControl.ReadValueFromBufferAsObject`.\ This\ allows\ reading\ a\ value\ stored\ in\ memory\ without\ having\ to\ know\ the\ value\ type.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ New\ processors:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ *\ \`{}ScaleProcessor`}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ *\ \`{}ScaleVector2Processor`}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ *\ \`{}ScaleVector3Processor`}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ *\ \`{}InvertVector2Processor`}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ *\ \`{}InvertVector3Processor`}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ *\ \`{}NormalizeVector2Processor`}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ *\ \`{}NormalizeVector3Processor`}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ Added\ \`{}MultiTapInteraction`.\ Can\ be\ used\ to\ listen\ for\ double-\/taps\ and\ the\ like.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ Can\ get\ total\ and\ average\ event\ lag\ times\ through\ \`{}InputMetrics.totalEventLagTime`\ and\ \`{}InputMetrics.averageEventLagTime`.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \`{}Mouse.forwardButton`\ and\ \`{}Mouse.backButton`.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ The\ input\ debugger\ now\ shows\ users\ along\ with\ their\ paired\ devices\ and\ actions.\ See\ the\ [documentation](Documentation\string~/UserManagement.md\#debugging)}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ Added\ third\ and\ fourth\ barrel\ buttons\ on\ \`{}Pen`.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\#\#\#\#\ Actions:}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ Actions\ have\ a\ new\ continuous\ mode\ that\ will\ cause\ the\ action\ to\ trigger\ continuously\ even\ if\ there\ is\ no\ input.\ See\ the\ [documentation](Documentation\string~/Actions.md\#continuous-\/actions)\ for\ details.\ \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ![Continuous\ Action](Documentation\string~/Images/ContinuousAction.png)}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ Actions\ have\ a\ new\ pass-\/through\ mode.\ In\ this\ mode\ an\ action\ will\ bypass\ any\ checks\ on\ control\ actuation\ and\ let\ any\ input\ activity\ on\ the\ action\ directly\ flow\ through.\ See\ the\ [documentation](Documentation\string~/Actions.md\#pass-\/through-\/actions)\ for\ details.\ \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ![Pass-\/Through\ Action](Documentation\string~/Images/PassThroughAction.png)}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ Can\ now\ add\ interactions\ and\ processors\ directly\ to\ actions.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ![Action\ Properties](Documentation\string~/Images/ActionProperties.png)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ *\ This\ is\ functionally\ equivalent\ to\ adding\ the\ respective\ processors\ and/or\ interactions\ to\ every\ binding\ on\ the\ action.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ Can\ now\ change\ the\ type\ of\ a\ composite\ retroactively.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ![Composite\ Properties](Documentation\string~/Images/CompositeProperties.png)}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ Values\ can\ now\ be\ read\ out\ as\ objects\ using\ \`{}InputAction.CallbackContext.ReadValueAsObject()`.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ *\ Allocates\ GC\ memory.\ Should\ not\ be\ used\ during\ normal\ gameplay\ but\ is\ very\ useful\ for\ testing\ and\ debugging.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ Added\ auto-\/save\ mode\ for\ .inputactions\ editor.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ![Auto\ Save](Documentation\string~/Images/AutoSave.png)}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ Processors,\ interactions,\ and\ composites\ can\ now\ define\ their\ own\ parameter\ editor\ UIs\ by\ deriving\ from\ \`{}InputParameterEditor`.\ This\ solves\ the\ problem\ of\ these\ elements\ not\ making\ it\ clear\ that\ the\ parameters\ usually\ have\ global\ defaults\ and\ do\ not\ need\ to\ be\ edited\ except\ if\ local\ overrides\ are\ necessary.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ Can\ now\ set\ custom\ min\ and\ max\ values\ for\ axis\ composites.}

\end{DoxyCode}
 var action = new Input\+Action(); action.\+Add\+Composite\+Binding("{}\+Axis(min\+Value=0,max\+Value=2)"{}) .With("{}\+Positive"{}, "{}$<$\+Keyboard$>$/a"{}) .With("{}\+Negative"{}, "{}$<$\+Keyboard$>$/d"{}); 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item "{}\+C\# Class File"{} property on .inputactions importer settings now has a file picker next to it.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Trace} has seen various improvements.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Recorded data will now stay valid even if actions are rebound to different controls.
\item Can listen to all actions using {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Trace.\+Subscribe\+To\+All}.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Action\+Trace} now maintains a list of subscriptions. Add subscriptions with {\ttfamily Subscribe\+To} and remove a subscription with {\ttfamily Unsubscribe\+From}. See the \href{Documentation~/Actions.md\#tracing-actions}{\texttt{ documentation}} for details.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1213}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixes}{Fixes}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1213}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed support for \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} 2019.\+1 where we landed a native API change.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+User.\+Unpair\+Devices\+And\+Remove\+User()} corrupting device pairings of other Input\+Users
\item Control picker in UI having no devices if list of supported devices is empty but not null
\item {\ttfamily Index\+Out\+Of\+Range\+Exception} when having multiple action maps in an asset (\#359 and \#358).
\item Interactions timing out even if there was a pending event that would complete the interaction in time.
\item Action editor updates when asset is renamed or moved.
\item Exceptions when removing action in last position of action map.
\item Devices marked as unsupported in input settings getting added back on domain reload.
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Pen} causing exceptions and asserts.
\item Composites that assign multiple bindings to parts failing to set up properly when parts are assigned out of order (\#410).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1214}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Known Issues}{Known Issues}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1214}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Input processing in edit mode on 2019.\+1 is sporadic rather than happening on every editor update.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1215}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}0.\+1.\+2-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2018-\/12-\/19}{\mbox{[}0.\+1.\+2-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2018-\/12-\/19}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1215}
\begin{DoxyVerb}NOTE: The minimum version requirement for the new input system has been bumped
      to 2018.3. The previous minum requirement of 2018.2 is no longer supported.
      Also, we have dropped support for the .NET 3.5 runtime. The new .NET 4
      runtime is now required to use the new input system.
\end{DoxyVerb}
 We\textquotesingle{}ve started working on documentation. The current work-\/in-\/progress can be found on \href{https://github.com/Unity-Technologies/InputSystem/blob/develop/Packages/com.unity.inputsystem/Documentation~/InputSystem.md}{\texttt{ Git\+Hub}}.\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1216}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1216}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Configuration} has been replaced with a new {\ttfamily Input\+Settings} class.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+Configuration.\+lock\+Input\+To\+Game} has been moved to {\ttfamily Input\+Editor\+User\+Settings.\+lock\+Input\+To\+Game\+View}. This setting is now persisted as a local user setting.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+update\+Mask} has been replaced with {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+update\+Mode}.
\item {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+run\+In\+Background} has been moved to {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+run\+In\+Background}.
\item Icons have been updated for improved styling and now have separate dark and light skin versions.
\item {\ttfamily Lock Input To Game} and {\ttfamily Diagnostics Mode} are now persisted as user settings
\item Brought back {\ttfamily .current} getters and added {\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+filter\+Noise\+On\+Current} to control whether noise filtering on the getters is performed or not.
\item Removed old and outdated Doxygen-\/generated API docs.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1217}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1217}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+settings} contains the current input system settings.
\item A new UI has been added to "{}\+Edit $>$$>$ Project Settings..."{} to edit input system settings. Settings are stored in a user-\/controlled asset in any location inside {\ttfamily Assets/}. Multiple assets can be used and switched between.
\item Joystick HIDs are now supported on Windows, Mac, and UWP.
\item Can now put system into manual update mode ({\ttfamily Input\+Settings.\+update\+Mode}). In this mode, events will not get automatically processed. To process events, call {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+Update()}.
\item Added shortcuts to action editor window (requires 2019.\+1).
\item Added icons for .inputactions assets.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1218}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1218}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Input\+System.\+devices} not yet being initialized in {\ttfamily Mono\+Behaviour.\+Start} when in editor.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1219}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Known Issues}{Known Issues}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1219}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Input settings are not yet included in player builds. This means that at the moment, player builds will always start out with default input settings.
\item There have been reports of some stickiness to buttons on 2019.\+1 alpha builds. We are looking at this now.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1220}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\mbox{[}0.\+0.\+14-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2018-\/12-\/11}{\mbox{[}0.\+0.\+14-\/preview\mbox{]} -\/ 2018-\/12-\/11}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1220}
\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1221}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1221}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Pointer.\+delta} no longer has {\ttfamily Sensitivity\+Processor} on it. The processor was causing many issues with mouse deltas. It is still available for adding it manually to action bindings but the processor likely needs additional work.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1222}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__hey_tea_9_2_library_2_package_cache_2com_8unity_8inputsystem_0d1_86_83_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1222}
\doxylink{namespace_core}{Core}\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Invalid memory accesses when using .NET 4 runtime
\item Mouse.\+button not being identical to Mouse.\+left\+Button
\item Dual\+Shock not being recognized when connected via Bluetooth
\end{DoxyItemize}
